Minister of the Army Hayashi entered the residence at 9:45 PM and stated that because his younger brother, Shirakami Sakichi, had been convicted, and at a time when the issue of discipline was serious, he wished to set an example and had submitted a letter of resignation. He felt sorry that this case had occurred while His Highness the Chief of Staff was traveling, causing him to change his planned itinerary. Imperial Prince Kan'in immediately offered words of comfort, and the Minister of the Army left the palace at 10:25 PM. (Japan United Press dispatch on the 15th)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saitō is scheduled to enter the Imperial Palace on the 16th to meet with the Emperor and report in detail on the process by which Minister of the Army Hayashi submitted a letter of resignation due to being implicated himself, but was fortunate to have been unanimously persuaded to stay by the army and decided to withdraw his resignation. After answering questions, he will withdraw and return the retained letter of resignation to Minister of the Army Hayashi. (Japan United Press dispatch on the 15th)

(Tokyo) Viewed from the current political situation, Minister of the Army Hayashi's withdrawal of his resignation is quite appropriate, and all parties have expressed goodwill. The opinions of various parties are recorded as follows:

House of Peers: The Minister of the Army's decision to remain in office is due to the efforts of Chief of the General Staff Imperial Prince Kan'in and the entire army, which is truly a good thing. The Minister of the Army's firm will could not be carried out due to the complex situation within the army, making it difficult to assess successors, which can be imagined. Therefore, the Minister of the Army's internal relations seem to require even more effort. The resolution of this issue will require a considerable amount of time. However, since the problem within the army has been resolved, it should not directly affect the political situation.

Seiyūkai: It seems difficult to retain Minister of the Army Hayashi given his personality. However, due to the sincere persuasion of the Chief of Staff and the sincere persuasion of the entire army during the meeting of the three top officials, Minister of the Army Hayashi had no choice but to change his firm decision. Although Minister of the Army Hayashi could not carry out his original intention, given the current national conditions of Japan, it is believed that a loyal figure as the Minister of the Army, as the leader of the army, should adjust the military and ease the feelings between the military and the people in order to smooth the national administration. Therefore, the Minister of the Army's remaining in office is a welcome event for the country and for constitutional government. (Domei News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

The Disarmament Conference is Repeatedly Delayed

Small European Countries Gradually Become Impatient: Sweden Sends Memorandum to the League of Nations; Urging Early Implementation of Disarmament Treaty; Baldwin Acknowledges Difficulties in Resolving Sanctions Issue 31

(Geneva) Small countries can no longer tolerate the delay of the Disarmament Conference. This is evidenced by the movement initiated by Sweden. It is heard that Sweden has sent a memorandum to the League of Nations, urging the speedy holding of the Disarmament Conference and the conclusion of a treaty. The treaty limits certain armaments, and concrete solutions are left for later. Naval disarmament will be discussed next year. It is also heard that the Netherlands, Denmark, Norway, Spain, and Switzerland have all endorsed the proposals in the Swedish memorandum, which will be considered by the main leadership meeting of the next Disarmament Conference. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(London) Lord Privy Seal Baldwin delivered a speech to voters in Worcestershire, discussing the issue of disarmament. He stated, "The current situation is chaotic and difficult to resolve. To establish an agreement to limit the armaments of various countries, and at the same time not to establish another agreement to sanction countries that sign the agreement but do not abide by it and increase their armaments beyond the limits set by the agreement, this is an extremely difficult problem to resolve. However, I believe that there is still hope of reaching an agreement on this matter. However, given the current situation in Europe, there are still various major difficulties. I must tell you these things in advance. I hope you will be patient and believe that the government will do its best to seek an agreement with various countries." (Havas News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

Maintaining the Balance of Power in Europe Depends on Understanding Between Britain and France: Lord Rothermere Advocates Returning German Colonies 32

(London) Lord Rothermere spoke to journalists in London today, discussing the relationship between Britain and France in the disarmament issue, the Treaty of Trianon, and the return of German colonies. Lord Rothermere said that given the current state of negotiations on the disarmament issue, the completion of maintaining the balance of power in Europe depends on the understanding between Britain and France. However, this understanding is not a united front against Germany. The Treaty of Versailles is the most unfair and evil act. The only way to remedy it is to return all of Germany's former colonies. The Treaty of Versailles stated that Germany was incapable of governing its colonies, and it is now known that this statement is untrue. Therefore, regardless of the position, this issue cannot be examined in detail. No one can doubt that Germany cannot possess colonies. Finally, Lord Rothermere stated that he supports the fascist movement in Britain because he believes that this movement is conducive to the revival of British parliamentarianism. (National News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

British Budget to be Presented to the House of Commons Tomorrow: Financial Revenue and Expenditure Shows Surplus; People Eagerly Await Tax Cuts 33

(London) The British people are now waiting for Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain to present his third budget to Parliament on Tuesday afternoon. When the financial situation is not good, the people do not expect tax cuts, so they do not pay much attention to the budget. But today it is different. Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain has achieved a significant surplus in the past fiscal year, which has raised expectations for tax cuts. Civil servants, as well as naval, army, and police personnel, all hope that the Chancellor of the Exchequer can at least restore part of the salary reductions made two years ago, and the people also expect the Chancellor of the Exchequer to reduce their income tax burden somewhat in the coming year. It is expected that the gallery seats in the House of Commons will be full on Tuesday afternoon. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

German Commercial Policy: Planning to Abandon Economic Self-Sufficiency; Control Import Trade 34

Hamburg German Foreign Minister Neurath announced Germany's future foreign trade relations and Germany's new commercial policy in a speech at an annual meeting banquet of a certain society tonight. According to the Foreign Minister, Germany's goal in the future is to restore the prosperity of the German ports of Hamburg and Bremen. These ports, due to their convenient geographical location, were previously centers for foreign commodity trade, but since the Great War, incidents have occurred repeatedly, and their commercial status has plummeted. The future of German commerce will be based on the following two points: ㈠ Abandoning the policy of economic self-sufficiency. I believe that no one in the German government dares to believe that the German economy should be isolated from foreign countries in order to survive. United efforts will make our nation and our economic system healthier day by day. Abandoning the previous reliance on foreign food and raw materials for self-reliance, significant progress has been made, especially in Germany's ability to be self-sufficient in food. Furthermore, given Germany's position in Central Europe, it is even more necessary to have close commercial relations with neighboring countries, especially the need to import raw materials, and it is urgent to establish friendly relations with neighboring countries. As for the second point, import trade will be more controlled in the future. Germany has to adjust import and export trade due to the impact of currency devaluation in various countries. Germany also purchases raw materials from those who buy refined products from Germany. Therefore, trade will be generally controlled by the government in the future, and individuals will not be allowed to make decisions on commercial policy freely. To achieve this new commercial policy, it depends on the stability of the international political situation. However, Germany is confident that it stands on the side of justice and will be able to achieve this goal. (National News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

Germany States Inability to Repay Debt: Meeting of Creditor Nations Called for Specified Date 35

(Berlin) The Central Bank has recently sent out invitations to convene a meeting of Germany's major creditor nations on the 27th of this month. French Civil Servants Demonstrate Against Salary Cuts: Postal and Telecommunications Workers Stage Slowdown; Disciplinary Action of Suspension; Government Issues Five New Ordinances: Reducing Veterans' Benefits 36

(Paris) The National Federation of Civil Servants has consistently opposed the government's delegated legislative orders on economizing government expenditures and will distribute one million leaflets to protest. The Federation has decided that civil servants in 140 cities across the country will march in demonstrations this Sunday, and all agencies will stop working for a moment next Monday to express their determination to undermine the government's deflationary policy. (Havas News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

(Paris) Taxpayers will take direct action against civil servants' demonstrations against salary cuts. Postal workers began a one-hour strike yesterday, and today a taxpayers' union with 500,000 members issued a declaration stating that if no immediate measures are taken to make the administrative agencies function, members will be ordered to stop paying taxes in order to avoid using them to support personnel who do not fulfill their duties and are not forced to fulfill their duties. Twenty-nine leaders of yesterday's postal workers' demonstration have been temporarily suspended, but today there was renewed demonstration at the Central Telegraph Office. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(Paris) Minister of Post and Telecommunications Mallarmé has recently decided on the punishment measures for personnel in the postal and telecommunications agencies who stage slowdowns. A total of 19 officials, one chief inspector, and one deputy inspector have been dismissed. As for the personnel who instigated a work stoppage and caused trouble at the Grenelle Street telephone exchange yesterday, they have also been transferred separately. This morning, Mallarmé personally went to the telephone exchange to inspect it and instructed the director to commend the personnel who were on duty as usual. Since this morning, the work in the exchange has returned to normal. (Havas News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Paris) Today, President Lebrun signed five new delegated legislative orders, stipulating measures for veterans to cooperate with the government and voluntarily reduce the receipt of benefits. Prime Minister Doumergue submitted a report stating that the budget deficit totaled 4,000,000,000 francs. The government issued 14 delegated legislative orders on the 4th of this month, which saved 2,800,000,000 francs. The five new ordinances issued today will save another 1,200,000,000 francs. The two orders have fully compensated for the budget deficit. According to the 14 orders on the 4th of this month, which canceled concurrent positions and reduced civil servants' salaries, the five new ordinances signed today ㈠ Prevent fraud, ㈡ Revise the amount of alimony for veterans' families, ㈢ Reformulate the method of free medical treatment for veterans, ㈣ Revise the amount of veterans' pensions, ㈤ Veterans voluntarily reduce various benefits by 3%. Overall, the measures to reduce government spending are of great importance. After the financial rectification, not only will the budget be restored to balance, not only will the currency be stabilized from then on, but the people of the whole country will work together to reduce the standard of living. In the short term, the general deflationary situation can also be seen in reality. (Havas News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

Six Important Bills Before U.S. Congress: Roosevelt Asks For Early Vote; Hopes for Passage of Tariff Bill; Silver Coinage Bill Unlikely to Pass 39

(Washington) President Roosevelt decided today to urge both houses of Congress to pass at least six major bills during this session. This decision was made after a three-hour meeting between the President and Senate leaders at the White House this afternoon. During the White House meeting, various bills already submitted to Congress were reviewed. According to the White House, the President hopes that Congress will vote on the following bills: (1) currency issues, (2) reciprocal tariffs, (3) tax revenue, (4) Federal Deposit Insurance, (5) municipal bankruptcy, and (6) Securities Exchange Control Act. The White House statement did not elaborate on currency issues, but according to the Associated Press, the government has not specifically designated any particular bill, but hopes that the Steagall Bill will be passed to address the financial situation. Furthermore, some sources interpret that the government hopes to pass a moderate silver bill to quell the opposition of the silver bloc. However, the proposed silver coinage bill is not expected to pass. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has consulted with Democratic leaders regarding the adjournment of Congress. Although the President is eager for Congress to adjourn early, there are certain issues that he considers to be of primary importance and he wishes Congress to decide on them as soon as possible. These primary issues are: (1) legislation authorizing the President to enter into tariff agreements with other countries based on reciprocal principles; (2) tax legislation; (3) legislation regulating securities exchanges; (4) currency legislation and legislation regarding the supervision of transportation industries. Among these bills, the President pays the most attention to the bill to obtain full power to conduct business negotiations. Roosevelt is extremely eager for this bill to be passed before the end of the Congressional session. It is also heard that among the currency bills there is a clause related to the silver issue, but according to senators and the press, the bill related to the silver issue proposed by the government is far from meeting the hopes of the pro-silver price increase faction in the Senate and the House of Representatives. The revenue portion of the appropriations bill, which was passed by the Senate yesterday, had an amendment attached that would increase revenue by $480,000,000. This amendment stipulates a three percent tax on Philippine coconut oil, which the President opposes and intends to veto to prevent. The leaders of the House of Representatives will meet with the President tomorrow to comprehensively discuss the bills that Congress has not yet completed, just as the Senate leaders did yesterday. Although these meetings are considering the procedures for the work before the adjournment of Congress, the date of the Congressional recess has not yet been determined, and even the approximate date has not been discussed. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Washington) Today, inflationists in Congress secretly circulated a petition seeking the House to pass the Goldsborough-Renneck Resolution. The resolution stipulates the issuance of paper money to clear farm mortgages. According to reliable information obtained by the Associated Press this morning, the petition has now been signed by 131 members, and fourteen more are needed to satisfy the statutory number to force a vote on the bill. The bill was introduced in the Senate by Republican Senator Goldsborough, and in the House by Representative Renneck. The bill stipulates that government bonds representing agricultural products shall be the guarantee for the issuance of this paper money. According to some currency inflationists, the purpose of distributing the petition is to counter the obstruction of the bill by the hard-money faction. (National News Agency dispatch, 14th)

Trotsky Hides in the Suburbs of Paris; Six People Living Together; Mysterious Movements; Police Investigation Reveals the Truth 42

(Paris) Police searched the Barbezon villa near Fontainebleau yesterday and discovered that Trotsky, the leader of the Soviet Russian extremist party, was hiding there. There were six people living with him, and their movements were mysterious. Only two people went out, while the others remained in seclusion. Every day, someone on a motorcycle came to the villa to deliver letters. One day, the motorcycle broke down halfway, and the police came forward to question him. The person was unwilling to reveal his name, so the police followed him and discovered that Trotsky was living there, holding a passport issued in 1933, with no irregularities. The prosecutor believes that there is no need for further investigation. Trotsky claimed that he was hiding here for fear of retaliation from the White Russians. When the police entered the villa to investigate, they saw Trotsky sitting at a desk on the top floor, with two very large pistols placed on the desk. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Conspiracy in Romania; Assassination Plot Against the King Carefully Planned; Unexpectedly Failed at the Hands of a Servant 44

Bucharest: Officers from Outer Transylvania secretly plotted to assassinate King Carol of Romania and kidnap his girlfriend, Madame Lupescu. They rented a house to live in at a location along the route that the King would take to attend Easter services at the church. The house was situated high, offering a distant view of everything. A servant of one of the officers was packing his luggage, placing several bombs in a leather suitcase. The servant was initially unaware of the plot, but later chatted with a soldier he knew, saying that his master's behavior was strange and that the leather suitcase was filled with heavy objects. This news was subsequently passed on to senior officials, who sent personnel to search the officer's room, where they discovered the bombs. World Animal Day; Global Publicity Efforts 45

World Society reports: The London branch of the World Society for the Protection of Animals recently published a report on the publicity efforts and commemorations in various countries around the world for World Animal Day, October 4, 1933. Key excerpts are translated below: Newspaper publicity for this year's festival has greatly increased. Many newspapers carried lengthy articles on animal protection. Greece participated in the commemoration of Animal Day for the first time. The London branch sent 140 letters to newspaper editors, requesting the cooperation of opinion leaders, and also sent special letters to social workers all over the world. The National (British) Society for Animal Welfare notified hundreds of elementary schools, requesting their principals to raise students' awareness of animal protection on that day.

Speedy Recovery After Airplane Ride 49

St. Louis: A young woman here suddenly suffered an acute illness, and her functions were almost completely lost. She became deaf, mute, and blind at the same time, lasting for six days. Her relatives and friends put her on an airplane and took her to the hospital in Lambert Field. While the young woman was unconscious, she vaguely felt as if the plane was falling from a height of 2,000 feet. Unexpectedly, just five minutes after the plane landed, the young woman's senses were fully restored, and she laughed and talked like a normal person. Everyone was amazed. The young woman, Mrs. Fowgyn, is 28 years old. When Mrs. Fowgyn was ill, her husband hired many neurology specialists to treat her, but to no avail. Later, she heard someone say that flying downhill in an airplane could cure the disease, so she tried it, and it worked miraculously. Mrs. Fowgyn had never been on an airplane before, and the airline initially refused to take sick people on board. Later, the company manager, Mr. Robertson, rode with her. According to Mr. Robertson, when the plane took off, the sick woman went into a coma. Afterwards, Mrs. Fowgyn told people that she would never hesitate to fly on an airplane again, and would first try riding in an elevator. Mrs. Fowgyn's illness was caused by a fall she had several years ago. (National News Agency dispatch, 14th)

Murder for Money Case Occurs in Tianjin 58

Overview of Construction in Chahar Province 72

Zhangjiakou, located at the southern station of the Chahar Railway, was changed to Chahar Province in the 17th year of the Republic of China. The provincial capital was established here, and the county name was changed to Wanquan. The city is divided into four districts: Shangbao, Xiabao, Kouwai (outside the pass), and the commercial port. Kouwai is inhabited by Mongolian merchants and a small number of Russians, while the rest are Han Chinese merchants. The city covers an area of ​​four li from east to west and more than ten li from north to south, with a population of approximately 120,000. It connects to Outer Mongolia in the north, entering Siberia; it passes through Duolun to the east, entering the four eastern provinces; and it heads west to Sui, Ning, and Xinjiang. It is a major gateway between the interior and the border regions. With Outer Mongolia's independence and the loss of the four provinces, followed by the crisis surrounding Duolun and Zhangjiakou, it is feared that according to Japan's Tanaka Doctrine, after the four eastern provinces fall into their control, eastern Inner Mongolia like Chahar, and western Inner Mongolia like Suiyuan, will also be regarded as delicacies to be seized. This goes without saying. Recently, the Japanese 80th Division in Rehe was transferred back to Japan, replaced by the 70th Division. There are reports that the command headquarters will be located in Duolun. In addition to the Zhang (jiakou) - Duo (lun) highway, the Japanese and puppet forces are also repairing the Duo (lun) - Gu (yuan) road, and have built airfields and stockpiled food in key locations. In recent days, Japanese suddenly came to Zhangjiakou to establish a Japanese-Chinese foreign firm, but its intentions are unknown. The next day, I visited Song Zheyuan, Chairman of Chahar Province, and Qin Dechun, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, and briefly discussed the political situation in Chahar Province as follows:

Qin Dechun on the Left, Song Zheyuan on the Left 73

After the end of the war in North China, Song was transferred to govern Chahar. The first step was to reorganize the mixed-brigade troops stationed there. He immediately followed the central government's order to reorganize and reorganize the various units of Tang Yulin, Huang Shouzhong, Li Zhongyi, etc., totaling about 200,000 men. He completely relieved the burden of local food supplies, dispatching firewood, and other responsibilities from the people, in order to appease the people and stabilize the region. The second step was to reassure the officials and people of Chahar. Any official found to be corrupt, as well as chiefs of public security bureaus, district chiefs, etc., engaging in interference in government matters or illegal acts, will be severely punished immediately upon discovery. Currently, a certain public security bureau chief is still in custody. He is also striving to eliminate excessive taxes and benefit the people. In terms of public security, the ten counties of Xuanhua are peaceful and tranquil. The five counties of Zhangbei (Duolun and Guyuan, where two to four districts have already been occupied by Japanese and puppet troops) have slight bandit activity. Zhao, the division commander of the 32nd Division, is determined to completely eliminate the bandits within two weeks. Sun Dianying's remnant troops, led by Yang Xiaohouzi, are attempting to flee eastward from the Suiyuan-Ningxia border, and precautions are being taken to intercept them. It is still easy to manage. If unfortunately there are border police or foreign troubles, it is his duty to follow the instructions of the central government and properly deal with them. The entire Chahar Province has a total of sixteen counties (including Duolun). The six counties outside the pass are high plateaus, flat and convenient for transportation. The ten counties inside the pass are full of mountains and rugged roads. Transportation, water conservancy, agriculture, industry, mining, and land reclamation all urgently need development. Li Yishan, the section chief of the Construction Department, gave a very detailed account of the construction situation since the establishment of the Construction Department. The following is a brief record:

In terms of transportation, the completed highways include the Zhang (jiakou) - Ku (lun) Road, Zhang Bai (lingmiao) Road, Zhang Duo (lun) Road, Zhang Bei (zimiao) Road, and Zhang Ping (Beiping) Road. The Zhang-Ping Road has no freight transport due to the impact of the Ping-Sui Railway. The Zhang-Ku and Zhang-Duo roads have been closed since the incidents in Kulun and Duolun. There are seven telephone lines: Zhang-Bin (chang), Xuan (hua)-Yan (qing), Zhang-Gu (yuan), Zhang-Chai (goubao), Xi (malin)-Huai (an), Xuan-Yang (yuan), Xia (huayuan)-Wei (xian).

In terms of water conservancy, Chahar Province is located in the northern frontier, with undulating barren mountains and little rainfall. It is urgent to find ways to dig canals and wells to supplement the lack of rainfall. Only Huailai, Wanquan, and Zhuolu counties in the entire province occasionally open canals to draw water to irrigate farmland. Recently, the canal at the border between Wan and Huai counties has been completed. The rest are lacking in both natural resources and manpower. Song advocated for the construction of wells. The Construction Department purchased well-drilling machines and distributed them to various counties for drilling. However, due to the geological composition of phosphate rock, no results were achieved. Seventeen new wells were drilled in Huailai, with water levels as low as tens or even twenty feet. Extraction is quite difficult, but for the sake of irrigation, it is still necessary to continue drilling.

In terms of agriculture, Chahar Province is located adjacent to the Mongolian plateau, with sandy soil and a climate of drought and little rain in spring and summer, and wind and snow in autumn and winter. Agricultural development is most difficult. Especially in the outer pass, cultivation is purely naturalistic. After planting, it is left to grow on its own, with no attention paid to cultivation and protection. The harvest is always less than in the inner pass. Currently, the provincial agricultural and forestry experimental farm is being reorganized and expanded, and plans are being made to carry out agricultural extension work, improve seeds, fertilizers, soil, etc. The counties are instructed to establish seed exchange stations and hold agricultural product review meetings in stages to study methods of preventing and treating diseases and insect pests.

In terms of forestry, the natural forests of Chahar Province have been completely harvested in recent decades. Moreover, due to poor climate and soil, it is difficult for trees to survive when planted. No attention has been paid to afforestation in the past, resulting in bare mountains and desolate landscapes. Now, all localities have been instructed to plant a tree per person, replant in autumn if it dies in spring, and pay attention to protection. According to statistics, the average number of trees planted and survived in each county in the past two years is approximately one million. In the future, the province's sixteen counties will be divided into three forest areas according to their terrain, and dozens of county and district nurseries will be expanded.

In terms of land reclamation, the wasteland outside Chahar Province, from the time when Yigu, the Minister of Land Reclamation in the late Qing Dynasty, released land for reclamation, to the time when the Land Reclamation General Bureau was abolished in the 16th year of the Republic of China, has almost completely surveyed and released the large tracts of virgin land of the Eight Banners and ordinary wasteland. At that time, people had already contracted to receive wasteland, paid the price according to the grade, and were issued certificates, and the property rights began to be determined. Other uncultivated wasteland will be surveyed and released separately after the investigation is clear, in order to develop land and benefit the people.

In terms of animal husbandry, the six counties outside Chahar Province and various parts of the Xilin Gol League have a sparse population and vast land, with abundant water and grass, making it a natural and prosperous area for animal husbandry. In the most prosperous era of animal husbandry in the former Qing Dynasty, the annual output was more than 5 million sheep and more than 400,000 famous horses. Even the number of sheep raised in each county within the pass averaged 20,000 to 30,000.

The Grandeur of the Qinghe Bridge in Zhangjiakou 74

Page 10

or more. In recent years, the local area has been unstable, and soldiers and bandits have been frequent, affecting animal husbandry, which has been declining day by day. The Provincial First Livestock Farm has now been established in Zhangbei County to raise high-quality breeding livestock, breed them according to law, and prepare for promotion and improvement.

In terms of mining, coal mines in Xuanhua, Weixian, Huailai, Zhangbei and other four counties have the most abundant output, followed by Huai'an and Guyuan. According to surveys and statistics, the area of coal mining areas in the province is approximately 135,350 hectares. Iron ore is also abundant in Xuanhua, Longguan and other counties, but it has not been formally mined. The same is true for sulfur mines. Methods of improvement: 1) Establish a mining consultation office; 2) Investigate mineral products; 3) Promote new methods of mining; 4) Develop major mineral deposits.

In terms of industry, the industry in Chahar Province is immature. Although the raw materials produced are extremely abundant, it is a pity that they cannot be used. In the past, there were only rough handmade products such as felt blankets and felt hats. Only two small factories that have been registered are the Xuanhua Yumin Egg Beating Factory and the Weixian Xinmin Weaving Factory. The Construction Department has now instructed various counties to establish people's livelihood factories, separately promote family handicrafts, encourage the holding of exhibitions, and reward specialized technical talents. In terms of commerce, because the province borders Mongolia, commerce tends to focus on trade with Mongolians. The main imports and sales to various places are fur, mushrooms, and crystal. The main exports and sales to Mongolia are interior vegetables, cloth, and groceries. During the period when Zhangjiakou and Duolun were open to commerce, commerce was extremely prosperous for a time. After Kulun became independent and transportation was blocked, commerce fell into a slump. After the anti-Japanese military operations last year, Duolun fell and the Zhangjiakou-Duolun road was also blocked again, and commerce suffered another major blow. As a result, all industries were in decline and increasingly depressed. In the future, if we want to revitalize and restore, we should first reorganize transportation, appease Mongolians, and broaden our recruitment. Secondly, we should repair the streets and markets in the provincial capital, promote the new system of weights and measures in various places, and promote domestic goods. Only then can the future of commerce be hopeful.

Japan Will Conduct Large-Scale Air Defense Exercises in Dalian, with Live Ammunition Fired in the Air and on the Ground, and 30 Aircraft from the Kwantung Army Will Participate 75

Dalian Dispatch. In order to enhance its citizens' knowledge of air defense and clarify its importance, the Japanese government has organized an Air Defense Association and established branches in various important areas, which is proceeding very actively. Recently, the Japanese government, for the sake of air defense exercises, held an air defense exercise meeting at the Dalian Yamato Hotel on the 5th of this month. Attendees included Fortress Commander Kagayama, Staff Officer Tsutsumi, Major Bann, Captain Mitsuno, Dalian Branch Director Karasawa, Adjutant Nakane, Mayor Ogawa, Civil Administration Director Mikageike, General Affairs Section Chief Inoue, Dalian Police Chief Terada, Fire Chief Imai, Lieutenant General Takayanagi, Chamber of Commerce President Takada, South Manchuria Railway Director Yamanishi, Korean Bank President Yoshida, Mitsui Manager Abe, Mitsubishi Branch Manager Terada, Electricity and Document Section Chief Seta, and presidents and reporters of various newspapers. As a result, it was decided to conduct a fierce live-ammunition simulated war between the air and the ground, and to release poisonous gas. The details of the decision are recorded below:

Exercise Period: From June 20th to 24th, continuing for four days and nights.

Weapons Used: Six anti-aircraft guns, four searchlights, six anti-aircraft machine guns, with an additional ten, eight listening devices, and twelve aircraft were initially planned, and the Japanese Kwantung Army is preparing to participate with thirty aircraft.

Exercise Area: The entire Japanese Kwantung Army, but the port area is a specific area. Because it is associated with the navy, separate exercises will be conducted at the same time. However, the focus of the exercise is on the cities of Dalian, Piziwo, and Pu Dian. Radio will also be very active. Police boats will set up air defense observation posts on the sea.

Light Control: Taking Dalian as the center, the control area is planned to be south of the Kinshu Civil Administration Office, or the entire area.

Passive Air Defense: In addition to the active air defense implemented by the military, other security activities will be formed into teams by local officials and people.

Exercise Methods: Simulated fire, live bombing, machine gun live fire towards the ground, release of poisonous gas, anti-gas action, smoke screen, and others. (Tohoku News Agency)

The Old Nest of the Fang Bandits, Zhoufang, Has Been Recovered; the Army Will Advance to Destroy Hengfeng and Geyuan 76

Nanchang Dispatch. Zhoufang, located in the northern part of Guixi County in northeastern Jiangxi, is intertwined with Yujiang and Wannian counties. To the north, it can connect to Leping and Dexing, and to the east, it can enter Yiyang and Hengfeng. It is an important old nest of the Fang Zhimin bandit gang south of the Rao River and north of the Xin River, no less important than the former Moban Mountain and the current Hengfeng and Geyuan. However, due to the complex terrain and deep bandit influence, although it has been besieged and suppressed by the stationed troops in recent years, it has been regained and lost in quick succession, with soldiers and bandits alternating, forming a tug-of-war. Since Chen Tiaoyuan, Commander-in-Chief of the Reserve Army of the Five Provinces' Bandit Suppression Army, was stationed in Wuyuan and unified the command of the stationed troops on the borders of eastern Jiangxi, Anhui, Zhejiang, and Fujian, generals such as Zhao Guantao, Yu Jishi, Tang Huiyuan, and Liang Lizhu have all been placed under Chen's command. They were divided into four sides, east, west, north, and south, to encircle and suppress the Fang bandits. According to front-line news, Zhoufang, the origin of the pseudo-10th Army, has been completely recovered after troops stationed in Guixi, Yujiang, Wannian, Leping, and Yiyang counties were divided into multiple routes to encircle and suppress the bandits and defeated the Yu-Gui pseudo-independent regiment and other bandits. Zhou, the magistrate of Guixi, has rushed to Zhoufang with the army to build bunkers, gather refugees, provide disaster relief, and restore order in order to seek follow-up measures. Moreover, Hengfeng City is currently the base of the Fang bandits, and the headquarters of the pseudo-Jiangxi-Zhejiang Provincial Government and the pseudo-10th Army Corps are located here. The pseudo-Red Army schools and arsenals are located in the Geyuan area of the county. Chen Tiaoyuan is also making all arrangements and commanding the army to advance to destroy them, in order to quell the bandit scourge as soon as possible. (April 12)

Bandit News from Sichuan, Henan, and Hubei; Chiang Instructs Liu Xiang to Settle the Sichuan Situation Early; Henan and Hubei Border Defense Against Sichuan Bandits; Wang Ma's Remnant Bandits Flee to Southern Henan; Chen Jicheng Reports Victory by Telegraph 77

Hankou Dispatch. After the main force of the Sichuan bandits retreated to Tongjiang, the focus of the Sichuan bandit suppression military affairs has shifted here. However, there are still a few remnant bandits in the Nanjiang area, and both sides of the Ba River have not been completely cleared. The advancing armies are still inevitably somewhat constrained. Chiang Kai-shek recently sent a special telegram to Liu Xiang in Sichuan Province, instructing him to clear the remaining bandits and settle the Sichuan situation early. The telegram stated in brief: "After the recovery of Bazhong, most of the bandits retreated to Tongjiang, and a small part retreated to Nanjiang. The Li and Luo units are now guarding the key points in front of Bazhong. For the sake of annihilating them in victory, in addition to telegraphing to advance along the Nanjiang, and to clear both banks of the Ba River on the fourth road, and to encircle Tongjiang, I hope that you will urge the armies of all roads to settle the Sichuan situation early, so as to relieve the central government's concern about the west. " As for the way out for the Sichuan bandits, according to various sources, they will definitely flee to the borders of Shaanxi and Hubei. Once they cross the Bashan Mountains, they will be in Shaanxi. Northern Hubei is also adjacent to it, with deep mountains and dense forests, which are more self-sufficient than the counties in northern Sichuan. Chiang Kai-shek believes that transportation on the borders of Shaanxi, Hubei, and Henan is inconvenient, and military transport is difficult. Once there is an emergency, it will not be easy to dispatch troops. He has specially ordered that the border area highways be completed by the end of April. This transportation network starts from Junyun in Hubei, Tongbai in Henan, and Baihe in Shaanxi, and they are interconnected with each other and connected with the original highways in each province. Currently, the section from the county to Laohekou has begun to be open to traffic, and only the sections from Yunyang to Caodian and Shiyan to Baihe have not been completed and are being rushed to build.

He Chengjun recently went to Fancheng again within three days to sit in town. The original stationed troops in northern Hubei included the 41st Division of Zhang Zhenhan, the 50th Division of Fan Shisheng, and the 34th Independent Brigade of Luo Qijiang. The 82nd Division of Rong Jingfang has also recently followed orders to go there. Since the military strength on that side is thick, the defense will be more consolidated. The remnant forces of Wang You and Ma Xiyou in Henan were besieged and suppressed by various armies, sometimes together and sometimes separately. First, Wang's bandits were defeated by Zhang Fang's troops in Queshan. Ma's bandits traveled from Shangnan in Shaanxi, through Junxian Nanhua, Lijiaqiao, and Houpo in northern Hubei, and Heilongji in Xiangyang, to Tangxian in Henan, and joined Wang's bandits, fleeing to Xindian and Liudian, crossing Yexian and reaching Feng, deep into the hinterland of Henan. After being besieged and suppressed by Zhang Fang, Pang Bingxun and other troops, they split up and fled south. Wang's bandits suffered the heaviest damage and are now besieged in Dushu Town, Fangcheng. Ma's bandits fled from Dengxian into Hubei. Luo Qijiang led his troops from Zaoyang on the 13th to attack together, and joined friendly troops Tang Yang and other regiments, and engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits at Suiyangdian. The bandits fled to Wangjiacheng, and there was a tendency to flee along the Tongbai Mountains to Zhongxiang. Luo has sent troops to track them down and has telegraphed the garrison in Zhongxiang to prevent them.

The remnant bandits in southern Hubei previously harassed Ruichang, and Wuxue on the opposite bank was once threatened by them. After being defeated by the 3rd Column of the Western Route Army, Chen Jicheng telegraphed Hankou twice on the 14th to report victory. 1) The remnant troops of Gao's bandits sneaked to the Lijia Dam area of ​​Mainan on the 8th, with about a thousand people and only a few hundred guns, and came into contact with my Guo (Rudong) Division. The bandits initially resisted stubbornly. Later, my Li Zongjian Brigade joined the flanking attack from the right wing. Countless bandits were killed in this battle. On the 10th and 11th, the bandits came to harass again, so we met them with three-sided counterattacks, killing countless bandits and capturing more than 30 people, including Yuan Zhongda, the director of the pseudo-political department, and Yao Shunxun, the captain of the special service company. The remnant bandits fled to the Jiangxi border. In addition to telegraphed local garrisons and Qingxian volunteers to block them, I respectfully report. 2) As for the bandits who harassed Ruichang, since Deputy Commander Guo Rudong personally supervised his troops, as well as Liu Peixu's Brigade, Li Zongjian's Brigade, and Zhang Liansan's Brigade, after annihilating the pseudo-Red 7th and 8th Regiments, the pseudo-47th Regiment, the pseudo-3rd Division, the pseudo-9th Regiment, and the pseudo-Special Service Battalion were extremely embarrassed and fled in all directions. On the morning of the 12th, the 154th Regiment of Guo's troops pursued from Mailiyuan to Zoujiacun, and engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits at Maicaoyan for four hours, completely defeating the bandits, leaving more than a hundred corpses behind and wounding hundreds more. They also killed Wang Taibang, the battalion commander of the pseudo-Longhu Special Service Battalion, whose pseudo-status was still on the body, captured more than 70 people, and seized more than 100 guns. The bandits were cut into two sections. The pseudo-3rd Division, the 47th Regiment, and the remnants of the pseudo-8th Regiment fled to Huangqiao, while the pseudo-9th Regiment and the pseudo-Special Service Battalion hid in Qijiaji. At the same time, Deputy Commander Guo led the 153rd Regiment and the engineering battalion to Qijiatan in Qingling to intercept them, and captured more than 40 bandits, killing countless people, and seized more than a dozen Mauser pistols and more than 20 rifles. Our company commander Wang was injured. The bandits fled to Cao, and were intercepted by Li Zongjian's Brigade from Quanyan, and fled to Daijiabu in embarrassment. Deputy Commander Guo is still supervising the troops to suppress them in order to completely clear them. Chen Jicheng, the original Administrative Commissioner of the Second District, has been relieved of his post because he cannot take care of both bandit suppression. He has telegraphed Chiang to approve it, and Li Huiwu has been appointed to succeed him. The Special Commissioner's Office has been moved to Yangxin, and Chen Yasheng has also been appointed as the Director of the Daban Special Zone Political Bureau, and the organization will be established next week. (April 14)

Liu Guitang's Bandits Fled Northward from Changcheng, Dare Not Stay in Wulian Mountain for Long, and Plan to Go to the Seaport but Fear Interception 78

Jinan Dispatch. Liu Guitang's remnant bandits have been fleeing from Henan to Shandong for nearly a month, and have suffered heavy blows and losses. On the 11th night, the bandits sneaked to Chaohe in Zhucheng and fled westward across the river overnight, passing through Dongshangpo, Zaogezhuang, Doutou, Jiajiazhuang, Xinzhuang, Wangjiazhuang, to Laojuntang. To the north of this place is Wulian Mountain, a deep valley with dangerous peaks and cliffs. There are several caves in the mountain that can be used as a refuge. On the 12th, the central government's aircraft flew from Xuzhou to Ju County, refueled, and then flew to the area occupied by the bandits to drop bombs and bombard them. Whether the bandits have entered the mountains or not is still unreported by the aircraft. The street district chief of Rizhao County reported that, according to refugees who escaped from Sanguan, Liu's bandits once sneaked from Wulian Mountain to Sanguan, and then returned to Wulian Mountain. This place is on the border of Zhucheng, 50 li away from Rizhao. Tang Bangzhi and Ma Guanyi's brigades have arrived in Rizhao by car from Ju County and are deployed in the south to block the bandits. Li Xuande's cavalry regiment and Wu Yuanxing's regiment are chasing behind the bandits. Gu Liangmin was stationed in Linyi, and Zhan Shutang previously led his Yun Qichang Brigade to Hongshiya to block them. Now that Liu's bandits have entered Wulian Mountain, Zhan led his pistol team to Jinan by car from Gaomi on the afternoon of the 12th, and Yun's brigade also returned one after another.

Wulian Mountain is a famous scenic spot in Zhucheng. The mountains are steep and dangerous, with cliffs and precipices everywhere. Only one road can pass through the middle. There are many azaleas in the mountain. The beams of the Guangming Temple are all made of stone. There are 150 to 160 monks. Whenever they hear of bandits, they block the road with stones and have guns for defense. A few bandits dare not pass. Liu's bandits had previously sneaked into the area the year before last, so they are hiding there again this time. I wonder if the monks will resist the bandits again this time.

Also, Liu's bandits tried to flee around the Sanguan Wulian Mountain area on the 12th. The 29th Division's Li Xiangchen Brigade was ambushed there and intercepted them. The bandits were caught off guard and fled in confusion. Gao Lantian's regiment also rushed to join the fierce pursuit, killing more than 50 bandits, capturing more than 40 alive, and seizing more than 20 miscellaneous guns and more than 20 mules and horses. The bandits did not dare to stay in Wulian Mountain for long and fled eastward, passing through Weijiagou and Liujia Chahe, in the mountains of Luan, and passing through Yangjiaogou, Liujiagou, and Majiazhuang. At 3 pm, Xu Wenyao, the deputy division commander of the 29th Division, led his troops to intercept them, seizing a bandit machine gun (Maxim), more than 100 rounds of ammunition, and killing more than 20 bandits. The bandits continued to flee southeast, passing through Pihuwowo, Xiaogaomazhuang, Ale, and Sanlizhuang, and sneaked to Shengshui, 20 li east of Majiazhuang, at night. They originally planned to continue sneaking to the seaport (the area is only a few dozen li away from Ju Kou), but because four warships of the Third Fleet were blocking the Shijiusuo Ju Kou, and the army was about to arrive, they did not dare to approach the seaport. At 1 pm on the 13th, they fled north from Shengshui, passing through Shizilu, Da Shangzhuang, Xiao Shangzhuang, Furong Village, Da Liangmazhuang, Zhituowo, Durugou, Shangyagou, Yaojiagou, Dongzhuang, Gao Machi, Douling, Migou, Nanling, Kuangsha Ridge, Wangjia Ridge, and Laozhuang, along the west bank of the Baichi River, to Changcheng, 25 li northeast of Zhucheng City. At 4 pm, according to aircraft reconnaissance reports, the bandits did not stay near Changcheng, but continued to flee to the northwest. (April 13)

Fuzhou Commercial Crisis: All Pawnshops Stop Issuing Tickets, Stores in the City Close One After Another, Finance Department Decides on Relief Measures 79

Fuzhou Dispatch. The commerce of Fujian Province was extremely depressed last year. When the old lunar year ended and the accounts were closed, each store drew up an account to the pawnshop, and each pawnshop was unable to collect the goods from the loan, and was unable to return them. However, due to the excessive urging, they were afraid of causing a collapse of the account and turning into a disadvantage. They had to change the method and allow each store to change the owed account into a term note and extend it to the second day of the second lunar month of the old calendar this year to repay it. Now it has been overdue for a long time and the stores have not repaid it. Each pawnshop is in a bad market situation. Eighteen companies, including Tianquan, Yuanquan, Zifeng, Hengyi, Jiuhe, Quanyu, Henghe, Chongyu, Xinchun, Shengyu, Zichun, Tianji, Fuyu, and Longshen, unanimously decided to reduce the scope of the issuance of tickets, only engage in exchange, and no longer release money. Therefore, only paper money from the Central and China Banks is currently circulating in the market, and the silver market is extremely tight. The goods handled by the stores last year have all been sold out, and it is urgent to add new goods to Hong Kong and Shanghai, especially silk, Su Guang, Jingguo, and oil and grain, which are in urgent need of goods. Now, because the pawnshops are unwilling to lend money and there is no money to add goods, they have to open the door and sit and watch. However, the rent, salaries, electricity, and all expenses must be paid as usual, and they cannot be maintained. Stores are closing or going bankrupt one after another. Just taking South Main Street in the city as an example, since the first month of the lunar calendar, more than 30 stores have closed, with each store owing an average of about 10,000 yuan. In previous years, if you wanted to open a store on South Main Street, it was difficult to find a place without paying hundreds or thousands of yuan in moving fees. Now, there are empty houses, and the rent has been greatly reduced. Some have even been closed for more than half a year without anyone asking about them. The Fuzhou Chamber of Commerce, in view of the increasingly declining commercial situation, has not urgently raised relief measures. The entire city's commercial market will inevitably fall into a total bankruptcy situation. It has submitted a request to the provincial government to transfer 1 million yuan to the Executive Yuan for the Fuzhou Central Bank to use to relieve the Fuzhou market. Stores are allowed to borrow money from the bank with real estate, goods, or securities as collateral, so as to help the group. It has been many days since then, and no instructions have been received. The commercial market has entered a state of stagnation. Even the pawnshops, which have the closest relationship with the economy of the common people, have also proposed to stop pawnshops because the pawnshops have withdrawn the money and tickets and have no way to operate. (Now pawnshops do not accept items worth less than five yuan. Those worth five yuan can only be pawned for four or five corners.) Government taxes of all kinds have also been sharply reduced due to the commercial stagnation. For this reason, the Finance Department specially convened representatives of various banks and pawnshops on the 10th of this month to discuss relief measures and decided that the Central and China Banks would lend 500,000 yuan to the pawnshops, and the pawnshops would issue 1 million yuan in tickets, which would be used exclusively for circulating the market's finances. Stores are allowed to borrow money from the pawnshops with warehouse goods or bills of exchange as collateral for the purpose of adding goods. The detailed measures will be negotiated by the three parties of the bank, pawnshop, and chamber of commerce, and must be realized within a short period of time in order to relieve the commercial crisis. (April 11)

North China: The Decline of the Carpet Industry - Affected by Tariffs from Various Countries, Sales Sharply Decrease - More Than 500 Factories Now Only 80 Remain 80

Tianjin Correspondence: The North China carpet industry is a national private enterprise. Its products are sold overseas and enjoy a high reputation in Europe and the United States. During its peak in 1923, there were more than 600 factories in Tianjin and Hebei. The finished products were all wholesaled by European and American export companies. The annual trade volume reached a maximum of 20 million taels of silver. Taking Tianjin alone, more than 530 factories and over 30,000 workers were engaged in this industry. In recent years, due to increased tariffs in various countries and economic panic, carpets, being between decorations and luxury goods, have been subject to heavy taxes when sold to Europe and the United States. In the United States, the initial tax rate was 25%, later increased to 35%, and the year before last, it was changed to 55%. Last year, the tax was no longer based on the value of the goods but was levied at a rate of 55 taxes per foot, causing the sales of North China carpets to become precarious. Few Chinese people buy and transport this product; sales rely solely on Britain and the United States. In recent years, with the global economic panic, British and American people are also unable to afford them, and British and American machine-made products are also increasing daily, surpassing our North China products in beauty. Although the price is cheaper, and the sturdiness cannot match our Chinese handmade products, customers rarely discern this subtle point, and the sales of domestic carpets are also affected. Even in the domestic market, domestic products are not as popular as Western goods, mainly due to the high price of domestic goods. Recently, only more than 30 factories remain in Peiping and less than 90 in Tianjin. Among them, Qing Sheng Heng in Tianjin has relatively large capital. Three years ago, they had over a thousand workers. Since last year, due to business depression, they have reduced to 140-150 people. The total turnover for the year before last was more than 40,000 yuan, last year it was more than 100,000 yuan, and in the first half of this year, it was about 40,000 yuan, which is ten times less than the business income in the previous five years. Europeans and Americans used to order more than 10,000 feet at a time, but now they order at most 2,000-3,000 feet, and the price must be lowered. Now, the best carpets sold to the United States are about 1.8 yuan per foot. Because the US tariff is calculated by the foot, medium and low-grade goods cannot be shipped. The best goods sold to the UK are about 1.5 yuan, the medium grade is 1.2 yuan, and the lower grade is about 80-90 cents. At such low prices, factories can barely support themselves when business is booming. If there is a recession, they will suffer losses. Those that are not as large as Qing Heng have 20-30 workers. They first contact various foreign firms. If they have a buyer, they start work; otherwise, they stop, or the customer provides the raw materials and they undertake the manual work. Their income is sufficient to maintain operations. According to statistics, there are now less than 5,000 workers in this industry in Tianjin, several times less than in the past. Recently, the carpet industry association, seeing the industry in danger and on the verge of total collapse, has held repeated meetings to study rescue measures. However, this matter is not about the power of the national government. The tariff barriers of European and American countries have increased, restricting the import of our goods, and it cannot be effective unless diplomatic methods are used. Therefore, it is planned to jointly submit a petition to the government with the Shanghai Carpet Industry Association, requesting that the carpet be removed from the list of luxury goods. However, this matter involves a change in the tariff rate of a country, and it is feared that negotiations may not be effective. (13th)

Jiangsu Province Plans to Build the Tonghai Railway - Total Expenditure of More Than 70 Million Yuan, Shared by Government and Business - Construction to Begin in June This Year, Completion by the End of Next Year 81

Qingjiangpu News: Last year, the Ministry of Industry of the National Government and the National Economic Committee, etc., had planned to jointly invest in operating the Lianghuai Reclamation Zone to develop Jiangbei, but it was suspended due to lack of funds. Now, 12 people, including Rong Zongjing, a flour merchant, He Yingqin, Minister of Military Administration, and Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, have stepped forward to organize the Jiangbei Coastal Trust Group Farm, which has been specially approved by the central government to operate and invest in managing all farms, water conservancy projects, and all production undertakings along the coast of Jiangbei. They are now actively preparing, and it will soon be realized. Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, also regards Jiangbei as the source of wealth for the entire province. Last year, he formulated a three-year plan for developing Jiangbei based on the provincial treasury's capabilities and is now gradually promoting it. The primary issue for development is convenient transportation. It has been decided to raise funds to build the Tonghai Railway, which is expected to be completed in two years. The route starts from Nantong, passes through Dongtai, Rufou, Yancheng, Funing, Lianshui, Huaiyin, Suqian, Muyang, and Guanyun to reach Haizhou, connecting with the Longhai Railway. Shen Baixian, Director of the Construction Department, has been ordered to be responsible for the plan. After receiving the order, Shen invited many senior merchants and engineers from Jiangsu Province to form an inspection team to inspect the planned route. The team has now completed the inspection and submitted the details to the Provincial Department. After receiving the report, the province specifically ordered the county magistrates of Tong, Dong, Yan, Huai, Mu, Hai, and other ten counties to estimate the number and value of the civilian land mu along the route and report to the Provincial Government before May 10 for purchase. Three engineers from the Construction Department, Chen Ziding and Wen Zhengshi, were also dispatched from the province to survey the route. Chen and others arrived in Pu by car from Haizhou on the morning of the 12th. When reporters visited, Wen said that the province has formulated a three-year plan for the development of Jiangbei, and agricultural land and water conservancy are now advancing simultaneously. Industry tycoon Rong Zongjing and others have raised huge sums of money to create the Jiangbei Coastal Trust Farm in the Lianghuai salt wasteland. The province is now aware that without convenient transportation in Jiangbei, other undertakings cannot be carried out step by step. The development of transportation is the foundation for developing various undertakings in Jiangbei. The province has now decided to do its best to build the Tonghai Railway. This road is the main line of transportation in Jiangbei. We (Wen referred to himself) are ordered to resurvey the roadbed. After the ten counties of Tongdong, etc., report the number and value of the civilian land mu along the route to the provincial government for purchase, construction can begin. The entire road (from Nantong to Haizhou) is 470 li long, and the estimated cost is 71.1 million yuan, including 2.2 million yuan for land purchase, 35 million yuan for materials, and 33.8 million yuan for construction. Because this road passes through the Jiangbei Coastal Trust Farm, the transportation of farmland products in the reclamation area will be greatly facilitated after its completion. It will enable Jiangbei agricultural products to be transported to Haizhou to the north via this road, connecting with the Longhai and Jinpu railways, and sold to various provinces in North China. To the south, it can be transported to Nantong via this road, which has a great relationship with the rural commercial economy of Jiangbei. Currently, the Jiangbei Coastal Trust Farm has undertaken 40 million yuan in funding, and the remaining 31.2 million yuan will be raised by the Jiangsu Provincial Government. The Jiangbei Coastal Trust Farm's funds have been borrowed from foreign banks by Rong Zongjing and others, and the method has been agreed upon, and a portion has been allocated. Chen Chairman has managed to raise the 31.2 million yuan borne by the Jiangsu Provincial Government from the provincial treasury, which is in dire straits. The province has contacted the financial community in Beijing and Shanghai several times regarding the remaining 10 million yuan to borrow funds, using the province's special construction funds as collateral, and it is scheduled to be repaid in installments within five years. It is heard that the financial community in Beijing and Shanghai has agreed, so the funding is not a problem. The provincial government is now actively preparing and has decided to start building the roadbed in early June, striving to complete the roadbed by the end of this year and lay the rails and open to traffic next year.

Changshu: Major Fire on Siqian Street 82

Yongshunyuan Paper Shop, located at No. 44 Siqian Street in this county, has an unusually developed business and can be called the leader in the Changshu paper industry. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 14th of this month at 4 o'clock, a fire broke out and quickly spread. All the goods in the shop were flammable, and the flames lit up the sky for a time. The neighbors on the left and right, hearing the news, quickly got up to rescue, and because this place was located in a bustling street market, it was even more shocking. Fortunately, all the fire brigades arrived at the scene to extinguish the fire, and the neighbors were not affected, but all the goods of the shop were burned down, with losses of more than 10,000 yuan. When the fire was raging, the shop workers living upstairs could not escape because the wooden ladder had broken. Five people jumped out of the upstairs window one after another, and three were injured. One, named Zeng Xuan, was the most seriously injured and has been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Male Corpse Found by the River 83

An unnamed male corpse was found in the Yemaokou area of Xizhoushi in the old Tenth District on the morning of the 14th. He was about thirty years old, wearing a blue cloth cotton robe and black trousers, and seemed to be a merchant. The nearby villagers reported to the village chief, who had the corpse retrieved, but the face was slightly rotten, making it difficult to identify the appearance for a while. In the afternoon, an old man came, claiming to be surnamed Xu. After carefully identifying the corpse, he said that the deceased was his son-in-law. Because he had lost his wife last year, he was depressed and unhappy, and his nerves were greatly stimulated. This time, he may have committed suicide by drowning.

Wuxi: Bureau Chief Sentenced to Imprisonment for Corruption 84

Qiu Jiusheng, former Director of the Changxi Smoked Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Bureau, was dismissed from his post and sent to the County Court for interrogation and detention for dereliction of duty, embezzlement, and corruption for personal gain. Yesterday, Judge Liu opened the court to pronounce the judgment in this case. Qiu Jiusheng was sentenced to six months in prison for the crime of embezzlement. Qiu declared in court that he refused to accept the sentence. Judge Liu ordered him to be returned to custody. It is also heard that Zhu Shusheng, the inspector of the bureau, and Zhang Quanyuan, the accountant, also had embezzlement, and the court will make separate judgments.

Audit of Field Tax Completed by the Provincial Department 85

Zhao Dihua, Director of the Department of Finance, in order to rectify the abuses of field tax in various counties, specifically sent commissioners to various counties to thoroughly investigate the field tax situation. He discovered major fraud and embezzlement of silver and grain worth 100,000 yuan in Liyang and other counties, so Director Zhao paid more attention to this matter. On the 12th of last month, he sent Commissioner Wu Gengyu to Wuxi to work with the staff of the Field Tax Office to start auditing the version strings stored in the collection office and the silver and grain that had been collected to see if they matched. At the same time, the county government also sent Wang Guangyan and Sun Zhaolin, staff members of the Clearing and Measuring Voucher Office, to review and recalculate after each map was calculated in order to prevent abuses. From October 1927 to the latest first-term land price tax in 1933, the totals were listed and collected by year and by map. By the day before yesterday, the calculation was completed. It was concluded that the total number of version strings stored was the same as the amount of silver owed in the grain cabinet register, without any errors. And the silver and grain collected in this county, from 1915 to 1926, totaled 36 terms, which had been ordered to be exempted by the Department of Finance. After auditing the stored version strings, they were sent to the Department treasury for storage. Only 10% was owed each year. By 1924, the debt was slightly heavier. According to statistics from the two offices, there were more than 187,000 taels of silver and more than 93,000 stones of grain, with 1.65 million Guizi version string households and 1.3 million Yizi version string households. The detailed numbers of the stored version strings were written into a clear register by the Field Tax Office yesterday and reported to the County Government for filing. The version string registers were bound into 30 large boxes and immediately sent to the Department of Finance for storage.

Car Accident on Xiyi and Xicheng Roads 86

After the construction of the Xiyi Highway, it was exclusively operated by the Jiangnan Long-Distance Bus Company. At about 3:00 p.m. on the 14th, the company's No. 17 bus was carrying passengers from Yi to Wuxi. When it was driving near Xueyan Bridge, there was a child of ten years or so walking leisurely on the road. Seeing this, the bus driver immediately turned the car to the left to avoid him, but the child suddenly turned to the left at this time as well. In order to avoid hitting the child, the driver slammed on the brakes. However, the car was moving very fast and could not stop suddenly, so the car body fell to the left. At that time, there were more than a dozen passengers in the car, all of whom were panicked and lost their color. Fortunately, the driver quickly opened the car window, and the passengers were able to climb out. However, Pan Linfang (45 years old), Huang Lihe (39 years old), Zhang Jishi (55 years old), and others suffered serious injuries to their left cheekbones, foreheads, and hands. One, Pan Linfang, was the most seriously injured and has been sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Yesterday, a No. 169 business car on the Xicheng Highway also crashed into a rickshaw. A Danyang woman, Wang Zhengzhen (15 years old), a passenger in the car, broke her left shoulder bone, and Zhu Xiaoshenzi (28 years old), a rickshaw puller from Yancheng, injured his chest. Both were sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment.

Jiangyin: Escaped Bandit Murdered by Accomplices 87

On the evening of May 24, 1931, at around 7 o'clock, Shen Shenyan, the Catholic priest of Changshou Muyizhuang in the Ninth District, was kidnapped by bandit Cao Xiaotian and others. Cao has been executed, and his accomplice Xu Atang escaped to Jiashan, Zhejiang Province, and opened a noodle shop for a living. This time, he returned to his hometown to sweep the graves during Qingming, and was beaten to death by his accomplices in the Nansangshutian field of Bishan. He had been dead for two or three days. On the 13th, he was discovered by the villagers and reported to the District Office, which was transferred to the County. On the 14th, Inspector Shi Chen was sent to investigate.

Changzhou: Robbery Occurs in the Suburbs 89

More than a dozen bandits suddenly came to Chao Guibing's house near Dibatou outside Xiaonanmen, Wuyi, at about 1:00 a.m. on the 14th. They spoke with mixed accents, carried pistols, broke in over the back wall, broke open the door, twisted and beat the victim Chao Guibing, causing injuries to his head and waist. Then they searched and robbed more than 200 yuan in cash and dozens of pieces of clothing and jewelry. They took more than an hour to escape with the stolen goods. Afterwards, the victim reported to the Second Public Security Bureau and asked them to transfer the case to the county for strict arrest of the robbers.

Construction Department Announces Cooperative Statistics 92

Cooperatives in Jiangsu have become increasingly prosperous in recent years. According to the latest statistics released by the Construction Department, at the end of the 21st year, i.e., the end of June 1933, there were a total of 1,828 cooperatives distributed in 50 counties, with credit cooperatives accounting for 63.4%, purchasing cooperatives accounting for 4.32%, production cooperatives accounting for 13.7%, sales cooperatives accounting for 0.44%, utilization cooperatives accounting for 2.52%, and mixed-operation cooperatives accounting for 16.25%. There were 57,100 members, with a paid-up share capital of 453,580.01 yuan and an unpaid share capital of 100,808.50 yuan. Compared with the end of the tenth year (the end of June 1932), there were 1,721 cooperatives distributed in 50 counties, with 53,512 members, a paid-up share capital of 434,311.50 yuan, and an unpaid share capital of 100,296.50 yuan, showing improvements in quantity and quality.

Gaoyou: Brokers Protest Tax Collection, Request County to Recover 93

The Business Tax Bureau of this county previously sent personnel to the countryside to collect business tax. However, Zhao Yourong and Yang Helin of the Bali Song Cattle Trade, Gao Changwan of the Twenty Mile Pu Private Brokerage, and Qi Weiyin, etc. of the Cheluo Town Donkey and Mule Trade, refused to comply with the regulations and pay business tax. Director Zhang specially presented a petition to the County Government yesterday, requesting that the merchants be detained and ordered to pay the tax in order to maintain the national tax.

Qingjiang: Three Counties Survey the Lanqing Dam 94

At the junction of Huai, Lian, and Shu counties, Wang Youting, the technical director of Lianshui County, previously recruited laborers to build a Lanqing Dam in the autumn of last year, using it to block the water discharged from the Liutang River in Huaiyin. The villagers along the Liutang River in the Fifth District of Huaiyin were greatly dissatisfied and repeatedly submitted petitions to the former Eleventh District Administrative Inspectorate and the Provincial Government, sending personnel to survey the situation and defend their claims, but the matter has not been resolved. Recently, the villagers of Jinba Township in Muyang also spoke up for the people of Lian, saying that the dam must not be removed, otherwise not only would Lianshui be at the lower reaches and suffer floods, but also the farmland in Shuyang would be affected, resulting in a stalemate. Chen Yuezhong, Director of the Canal HuaiPi Section Works, was ordered by the province to conduct a survey, but was unable to go immediately due to being busy with the Liutang River project. The Huaiyin people could not bear it any longer as the flood season was approaching, and they dug open the Lanqing Dam a few days ago. The people of the three counties almost had a melee. Now the province has telegraphed Director Chen again to cooperate with the county chiefs of the above three counties to conduct a survey as soon as possible and resolve the matter quickly. After receiving the order, Chen has scheduled to go to the survey tomorrow morning (the 14th).

Complete the County-Wide Telephone Network on Schedule 95

Huaiyin County Chief Lu Cangen believes that the HuaiShu and HuaiSi lines of the county-wide telephone in this county have been installed, but the HuaiHuai and HuaiLian lines still lack funds for installation. Now that the summer flood prevention season is approaching, the telephone poles and lines are of utmost importance and should not be delayed any longer. Therefore, yesterday he specifically dispatched Zhou Boyou, Ding Wentao, and Wang Xiufu to various districts to urge the payment of donations, and appointed Qiao Shoushan to urge the Chamber of Commerce in this county to pay donations, deciding to complete the county-wide telephone network within the summer flood prevention period.

Xiaoshan: Continuous Rain, No Hope for Spring Flowers 96

In the past five days in Xiaoshan, there has been continuous spring rain and a sudden change in climate. Since the 12th, the temperature has dropped below 50 degrees. Due to mountain floods, the water in the Qiantang River has risen to the same level as the embankment. The water in the Xijiang and Beihai dikes has overflowed, rushing into the dikes, with more than ten breaches. The spring flowers outside the dikes are all submerged in the water, and the loss of farmland and sandy land is 100,000 mu. Looking outward from the dikes, the water is level with the river. The sand people's half-year income is completely hopeless, so the sand people have suffered from floods and are flocking to the inside of the dikes for refuge in an endless stream, which is very miserable.

Chairman's Report 101

After the ritual was performed, Tong Hangbai of the Presidium reported that all the representatives were able to participate enthusiastically and on time for today's Citizens' Representative Conference of the New Life Movement, which showed that everyone present had a considerable understanding of the promotion of the New Life. Since Chairman Chiang promoted the New Life Movement in Nanchang, the whole country has responded enthusiastically, and its efficiency is self-evident. Although most people have understood the meaning of the New Life, there are still many people who are alienated from this kind of movement. They only know its name but do not know its reality. Here is a brief summary. Our Chinese nation has always emphasized propriety, justice, integrity, and shame, but in the past 100 years, the discipline of life has tended to be romantic and decadent, so Chairman Chiang promoted the New Life to reverse this decadent trend and eliminate bad habits. If the people of the whole country can implement it according to the regulations, then the country can be expected to be strong, otherwise, even if there are no foreign enemies, it will be enough to lead to its demise. It must be known that the implementation of the New Life can relieve the worries and dangers of the country and promote the success of the people's cause. It is hoped that all representatives will encourage each other at any time to achieve implementation.

Yu Hongjun's Speech 102

After the Chairman's report, Yu Hongjun gave a speech on behalf of Mayor Wu Tiecheng, saying that the New Life Movement has been understood by all walks of life since its promotion. Its purpose is very simple. As long as the old morals can be maintained, the New Life Movement can be practiced. Some people in all walks of life do not understand it, thinking that the old life should be abolished urgently after the promotion of the New Life, but the purpose of the promoters is not like this. After all, the old life is not completely bad, and the New Life may not be perfect even after its promotion. It is not because the old life is bad that the New Life is promoted, so its main purpose is not to create a new way of life, but to maintain life with the old morals as the main principle of the New Life. All representatives, we only hear about meetings but do not see implementation. It must be known that in this extremely urgent period in our country, if everyone still holds on to the bad habits of laziness and ease, then the Chinese nation will have no way to save it. That is what is called despair worse than death. If all walks of life quickly realize the danger of the future, cultivate themselves, and pay attention to the implementation of the New Life in order to save themselves.

Lu Jingshi's Speech 103

Following that, Lu Jingshi gave a speech, saying that in this depressed society, it is easy to see that the fallen tend to fall further. Once those with aspirations graduate from school and step into society, they will inevitably be disappointed and discouraged, and all their expectations of how to develop themselves and how to serve society will turn to ashes, and they will instead tend to corruption. Those who are guilty of this should be held responsible. At this most dangerous time, we should jointly take responsibility to reform the bad habits in society, so that young people with aspirations will not be discouraged, but will strive forward, and everyone can achieve the purpose of cultivating themselves, managing their families, governing the country, and bringing peace to the world. That is, we want to create a militarized society for the people and reform all the corrupt atmosphere. This is the purpose of the revolutionary leader Chairman Chiang's promotion, but the biggest drawback of our people is not being diligent in practice, so in my humble opinion, the New Life, on top of moral sanctions, may as well be assisted by political power. After the speech, Zhu Xuefan, the representative of the General Labor Union, gave a speech (speech omitted). At 11:30 a.m., slogans were called, photos were taken, and the meeting adjourned.

Strict Alert 110

After learning that a large lantern parade would be held last night, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the Municipal Security Office, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched troops to various locations in the southern city to maintain order. The Municipal Public Security Bureau also ordered its district offices and inspectorates to increase manpower, dispatch personnel to maintain strict vigilance, and pay special attention to the parade route to prevent reactionary disturbances. The Municipal Defense Council ordered all team members in the southern city to be armed and on guard the night before to prevent incidents.
