How to Study Education (Continued) 178

— Answer to Wang Yin

Yesterday, we posed the question "What is the purpose of studying education?" to Mr. Wang Yin, and briefly explained the essence of modern education. Today, we present to Mr. Gan and all those preparing to become educators the attitude that an educator should take.

Editor

Of course, by saying this, we absolutely do not mean to neglect education or oppose the study of education. Education is one of the superstructures of society, and its development is certainly determined by the development of society, but at the same time, it can also influence and even promote the development of society. Our intention is only to correct the generally incorrect views on education and to indicate what education is at the current stage. To determine the purpose of studying education, without understanding the essence of education, without understanding the evolution of education, and wanting to recognize the trends of new education, there is no way to start. Moreover, we do not deny that under the current educational system, behind the privileged education, there are many hard-working educators who are striving for new education. This is just like in the capitalist system, there is a new force lurking that will destroy capitalism. Precisely because of this, we should not be blinded by vulgar educators, but should find our own way forward, abandon the education exclusively for the few, and strive for the growth of new education that can truly become the masses.

Under the natural law of social progress, the new education of the future will inevitably take a position opposite to the education of all stages before capitalism. The previous education was opposed to labor and was a tool for the few to control the people: the new education should belong to the masses and should essentially turn to combining with production. This is not like the general educators of today who emptyly shout "Education to save the country," but a natural product in a great social system reform. If this is understood, the proper purpose of studying education will not be difficult to recognize.

Now that we have a proper purpose, how should we begin our research journey?

Education is not only a problem that can be solved by theoretical exploration alone, but is also a practical subject. That is, just as studying physics and chemistry, it is not enough to remember a few formulas, but what is even more needed is experimentation. Therefore, for this question, we will temporarily divide it into two aspects.

Regarding theoretical research, in addition to education itself, as Mr. Wang Yin asked, what fundamental knowledge must be possessed when studying education? This is indeed the most important question for those who study education. Our answer is that the fundamental knowledge that must be possessed for studying education is necessarily social science knowledge. The reason for this is very clear. As mentioned above, the evolution of education is determined by a certain social productive force and production relations, so how do social productive force and production relations develop? Also, how is mental labor separated from physical labor? These are social science questions. If there is no deep understanding of these basic questions, it cannot be hoped that there will be any correct understanding of education. What should be particularly noted here is the knowledge of philosophy. Philosophy is the science of human life, the science that tells humans how to recognize material phenomena or psychological phenomena. We often hear educators raise the issues of educational psychology and mass psychology, but these issues cannot be answered by their subjective imagination. Therefore, you should first have a correct worldview, social view, outlook on life, and scientific observation method, and use them to study education in order to obtain correct conclusions. Here, we can introduce a book for preliminary study, which is the "Outline of New Education" edited by Li Haowu (published by Nanqiang Bookstore). This book can give readers a new understanding of education to some extent.

Then let's talk about the practical aspect. This is indeed a more difficult question to answer. The abolition of education and the emergence of new education integrated with production will inevitably have to wait until the new social system is on track. At this awkward time, it is not possible to go with the flow, and it is also useless to shout high-sounding slogans. What should those engaged in education do? We believe that the first thing to remember is that our education should always be a driving force for promoting social development, and should always be a motivator for enlightening the masses to learn on their own. Standing on this position, we begin our educational work. We can be teachers, whether in primary and secondary schools, or in literacy schools in factories and rural areas, but we will definitely not just be for life, not just shouting high-sounding slogans. We should understand the masses of students, and we should find the source of their distress in the real lives of the masses of students, and arouse their interest in reading and life. For example, the general vulgar educators now are suppressing the development of students' intelligence, but we are going to increase the development of students' intelligence and instill them with new knowledge as much as possible.

Our words end here, which is of course very insufficient, but if the readers can understand this clearly and use it as a starting point for studying education, it will naturally not be completely useless! (End)

Chunqiu

Fragrant Imperial Vapors 179

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shoujuan

However, she was indeed getting old; at that time, she was approaching seventy years old. Her face, her fingers, revealed the signs of old age like ordinary old women; but if someone bluntly said she was old, she could not help but be very annoyed and considered it a major insult.

"…Furthermore, they shouldn't say," she continued to mutter to herself, her anger gradually rising, "because there are things to be done here, we can't leave Beijing! Don't they even know that wherever our people go, the entire court will follow, and everything can still be done as usual? Like during the Boxer Rebellion in the year of Gengzi, when we went to Xi'an, the foreign soldiers couldn't keep up; and our court was still in our hands! Don't they even understand this? What do we need such stupid things for!"

Thus, the Empress Dowager's Eastern Tour was decided. The Imperial Astronomical Bureau picked a very auspicious date and time for our departure. On this day, the Forbidden City was filled with a frenzied and busy atmosphere, from Li Lianying to the lowest-ranking palace maids; from the ruling ministers to the smallest railway servants; from the Empress Dowager and her retinue to us, the attending ladies-in-waiting: everyone was equally busy.

Of course, the entire road from the court gate to the railway station had to be covered with a layer of yellow sand as usual; this yellow sand was soaked very wet, like the beaches by the sea, in order to prevent it from being blown away by the wind. As soon as we left the gate of the Forbidden City, we all got into sedan chairs: my sedan chair happened to be right behind the Empress Dowager's imperial carriage. We passed through the Zhonghua Gate, the Qianmen Gate, along Qianmen Street, all the way to Yongding Gate; that's where we boarded the train. (11)

White Grave 180

— Xiong Wan

Every time I pass Tongji Road, I always see that rectangular, whitewashed grave in a field by the road; on it are four large black characters: "Grave of Nomura," and a few small characters next to it: "×× Division Propaganda Group." Seeing it, the lingering images of the war in February of the previous year immediately appear before my eyes: my nose seems to still be filled with the smell of blood. And in my heart? It feels like I'm suffering a great shame.

However, the four characters faded day by day, and finally disappeared completely in these continuous days of spring rain. When I passed this road again today, the white realm was already a purely white grave. Lush green grass and golden little flowers grow all around. The fragrance radiates in waves, truly refreshing and evoking a feeling of "the beauty of early spring."

Who still feels the smell of blood? Who will still imagine the hand-to-hand combat...? What is shame? Everything has been carried away by time; washed clean by the spring rain. Enjoy it! Friends, this "beauty of spring"!

Tan Ci 181

— Yanzi

The most exquisite porcelain comes from the Kangxi and Qianlong eras of the late Qing Dynasty. In later generations, only the Hongxian era, when he deliberately sought refinement when Yuan Shikai proclaimed himself emperor, was comparable to the ancient porcelain of Guyuexuan. Researchers of ancient porcelain generally know this. Ge Jun Zufeng of Pinghu is good at calligraphy and painting and has a rich collection. He especially collects porcelain. Last summer, while recuperating in Lushan, he met He Xuren, a famous porcelain painting master from Nanling. Seeing the landscape on the porcelain screen he painted, it was exquisitely detailed and peerless. The snow scene was especially wonderful and divine, surpassing the painting templates of the Northern Song Dynasty Painting Academy, unprecedented, and breathtaking. Contemporary celebrities were honored to obtain one. Ge and He became friends for more than a month, often discussing ancient porcelain, and benefited greatly. He collected everything that could be used for reference for ancient famous porcelain. He said that the difficulty of painting porcelain is far from comparable to paper and silk. The color and glaze are thicker and coarser than glue and lacquer. Outlining is still possible, but dyeing is even more difficult. Moreover, the opening frame of the porcelain is only a few inches, and if you want the mountains and forests to be complete in the landscape, you cannot succeed without meticulous effort. How difficult it is to paint porcelain! He has Ji Kang's habit of not easily putting pen to paper. It takes several months to complete each piece. Most of the works of Xu Ren on the market are painted by his disciples, and Xu Ren occasionally touches them up. It is also heard that Xu Ren is unrestrained, values friendship, and has the demeanor of an elder. He indulges in the scenery and does not seek fame among the princes. He is truly rare and commendable.

Sculpting porcelain did not start today. What I have seen in the past, although skillful, lacked outstanding talent. If it is Xu Shunyuan's carving today, it is like a supernatural work, unique and extraordinary. Ge Jun obtained the rattan plate carved by him, as thin as a hair, the flowers are vivid and lifelike, and the colors are bright. At the Chicago Exposition, the dragon boat he carved was priced at 30,000 US dollars and was obtained by a Westerner. After the closing, he won the highest award, and the Westerners praised him as a unique skill.

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 182

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 27:闺怨暗中消慈怀可感/Silent Resentment Fades, Kind Heart Felt; 闲悉醉后起旧事难忘/Past Events Unforgettable Arise From Idle Inquiries After Drunkenness

These situations were first seen by Zhao Weng. He hid it from Guizhi, but quietly came to Jiang and asked: Dear Madam, I see that your grandniece always seems to be unwell. I want to find a doctor to take her pulse. What do you think? It is best to ask your grandniece. Otherwise, if you invite a doctor, and she doesn't let him see, it would be a joke. Zhao Weng had a pipe in his mouth, smoking one puff after another, but he couldn't help but reveal his teeth and kept laughing. Seeing his situation, Jiang also saw something, so he said: To tell you the truth, I have been worried about her for a while, and I have been watching her appearance, and I have been worried in my heart. If there is good news, then you have not pampered her for nothing. Hearing this, Zhao Weng was even happier, opening his mouth and unable to close it. Jiang also laughed; you are also attentive and see something. However, this child has a really stubborn temper. If you find a doctor again, she will be ashamed, and that's not good either. I think I will pay more attention from now on. For the past two months, the two old people have not had any jokes. Now Zhao Weng is constantly laughing, almost unable to hold the pipe in his mouth. Jiang's eyes were folded with fish tail wrinkles, as if the bursts of joy were surging from the heart straight to the face. Zhao Weng touched his beard and said: Dear Madam, although I am such a big age, after all, men and women are different, I think it is best to let her do less heavy work. Jiang then said: Old man, don't yell first, it's not certain. Let's wait for a while, and talk about it after this matter is clear. Zhao Weng said; although that's what you say, it's better to let her do less heavy work. Jiang laughed; okay, I'll find a chance to tell her, but it's still not good to tell her straight. Zhao Weng couldn't say anything else, just happy. (362)

Closer and Closer 183

Social Faces 184

— Yu Youqing

Mr. A is the general manager of the Suzhou ×× Association. He is born with a lively face, somewhat humorous. When he solicits members every spring, it is as if the spring breeze is on his face. When he sees people, he is very kind, bowing and making gestures, everything is available, and his face is full of smiles, more interesting and humble than the clown in Xiao Fangniu. But once the membership solicitation period of ×× has passed the end date, his face, like the weather in Huangmei season, gradually changes. First, he sees you, showing you a forced smile, then he sees you, staring at you blankly, and later, when the things he hopes for are successful, he sees you, not only not staring at you, but as if showing that he disdains to meet you, walking past you arrogantly. Maybe he thinks that you guys, "not big enjoyers, but small ghosts," who pay three or five yuan to become a member, what's the point? So the result is that he doesn't bother with you anymore. This is the three changes on Mr. A's face. But when next spring comes, his face, like Pei Skaden's performance, changes to Laurel and Hardy. Not only does he stare at you and smile, but sometimes when he sees you, Mr. So-and-so is long, Mr. So-and-so is short, flattering enough, his face full of smiles, making you feel more comfortable than the people who scrub your back in the bathhouse. His face comes with the spring breeze. I can't name it, so I call it: "Social Face."

Medicine Bag and Leather Bag 185

— Yang Yusheng

When a doctor goes on a house call, he always has to busy himself organizing a bag | called a medicine bag.

When a teacher goes to class, he also has to carry a bag | called a leather bag. It should really be called a book bag.

Of course, the medicine bag is filled with medicine. Medicine can certainly "save lives," but at the same time, it can also "take lives"!

The leather bag is filled with books. The books that can be taught are certainly mostly good, but it depends on how they are taught. If they are not taught well, the result is also equal to "taking lives"!

Casual Remarks 186

Research on Inkstones (20) (2) 187

— A Bored Guest

General Overview of Chengni Inkstones

(3) Ancient Bricks as a Type of Chengni: The above describes genuine Chengni inkstones. There is also a type of ancient brick called Chengni inkstone. Tang Tongyuan said of Chengni inkstones: “Baoshan in Tongzhou, Jiangnan, is also said to have Chengni inkstones. These are all made by locals from the sandy soil of Dachuan Sha and Xiaochuan Sha Huangyao and other places on the seashore, who dig up brick pieces. Some say that Lord Chunshen Huang Xie opened a kiln to make Chengni pottery here, hence the name Huangyao. However, from the Warring States period to now, it has been almost three thousand years, even if there was such a thing, how could broken bricks and pieces still remain today? It must be due to confusion with the Huangyao of the Ming Hongwu period. In the early years of Hongwu, Baoshan and Wusong were built as outer cities, and pottery was made at Huangyao, taking the fine, firm mud near the water of the beach to make bricks. At that time, the broken and discarded pieces were dumped on the beach. When the Baoshan city walls were submerged in the sea, the decaying walls and broken battlements were washed to the sea by waves and flowing sand, staying in the sea for many years, the fire nature completely disappeared. Locals obtained them and used them as inkstones, which did happen, but good ones were extremely rare. Merchants, officials, and gentry did not examine them carefully. Hearing that Tongzhou produced Chengni inkstones, they came to buy them. Every year in the third month, the Langshan incense pilgrimage and market gathering below the mountain were filled with stalls claiming to sell Chengni inkstones to deceive people. Passing guests could not distinguish the real from the fake and bought them at high prices, but they were actually made by stealing stone from Lingyan Mountain in Suzhou or searching for relatively old and fine bricks by the sea to imitate them." From this, it can be proven that the ancient city bricks of Baoshan in Tongzhou were also used as Chengni inkstones during the Qianlong and Jiaqing periods. Not only were the ancient city bricks of Baoshan in Tongzhou used as Chengni inkstones, but all ancient brick inkstones that could not be investigated were also called Chengni inkstones.

I have a duck-herding old man (Song Luo) bequeathed inkstone, Shao Changheng titled "Song Pit Rose Five-Color Chengni Inkstone", his postscript says, "Future generations discussing this inkstone, all consider it a Song pit Chengni, because Mr. Ran first made an inkstone, knowing it was to be treasured, but in reality, it is an old brick from the Qin and Han dynasties, unearthed in the Song dynasty." The duck-herding old man himself inscribed, "Dongpo Layman said that Chengni inkstones are divided into five colors, those from the Qin and Han dynasties are all red, which are of the highest quality, others are not as good. I have obtained this and can compare it to Juxuan jade."

I also have a wife Meixianguan inkstone, also known as a rose-purple Chengni inkstone, but on the side, the Yu Daoren inscribed: "Kunming robbery ash burns undead, coming out of the water still shines like electric purple, yin and yang furnace coal applies craftsmanship, but one knows not when was it molded, Xianyang one torch of fire virtue arises, no ruins of the Han family palace remain, to this day even an inch of soil is still precious, a thousand years of vastness mourn the Qing history, presenting alas the ancients underground cannot be awakened, ask of the traces of the Guan Chengzi," this is clearly saying it is an ancient brick from the Qin and Han dynasties.

From this, it can be seen that Chengni and ancient bricks were still not clearly distinguished by previous people, no wonder today's market appraisers randomly speak nonsense. In fact, Chengni and ancient bricks, if a little research is done, are easily distinguished. The manufacturing of Chengni is particularly fine and smooth. Even in terms of color, the red of its rose-purple is ultimately different from the red of fire-robbed bricks. Moreover, good Chengni often has interspersed shades of blue and yellow, and there are bean-sized sand, mung bean sand, halo of the moon, needle-tip silver stars, and other kinds of patterns, while ancient bricks do not have this type.

Page 15

Free Talk

Talking About Writing 188

— Xiang Li

Recently, it seems that many writers are discussing how to write. Some say to use quotations, others say to go to the streets. In fact, these can all be considered tedious, dispensable.

What is important is the thought, that is, the content of the article. Writing an article for the sake of writing an article is completely unnecessary. Of course, if there is something to say, one should try to say it in a way that moves the listener, and should have considerable skill. The writings of Berne and Shaw are vast and boundless, but claiming to be art for art's sake is not enough to move their writing one iota. The reason why they produce excellent articles is that they add a layer of sugar coating to bitter medicine, making it easier for the taker to swallow.

An article without content, even if it is written very beautifully, is of no use to the reader. Fleeting glimpses can never move people. Moreover, it is not easy to write. Just as speaking always expresses one's own opinion, how difficult is it to speak without one's own opinion?

When substance outweighs style, it becomes rustic; when style outweighs substance, it becomes vulgar. What is sought is to have "substance and style perfectly balanced." Ordinary writing practice is not for the sake of writing, but rather like practicing speaking, so that when there is something to say, it is easy to say, convenient to say. The purpose of "writing" is at most like this. And when one is eloquent, at this time, like light, like electricity, like the Yangtze River, the beauty of yang and strength, the beauty of yin and gentleness... all depends on the listener's association.

But it is rare to see articles with substance. Since the May Fourth Movement, there has been no shortage of people who can write, but many articles lack substance, resulting in emptiness. Even composing about the wind and moon requires one's own personality and thought, only then can the wind and moon be sentimental. Saying that young people's faces must be "pale," that the sky must be "azure," or that "heartstrings tremble," or "fists clench," all fall into the old trap of "writing for the sake of writing."

The number of people in front of our eyes who seem to write effortlessly is few, and even fewer can be said to have content. Many people wield guns and sticks, but have no unique skills, and only end up wandering in the world, dividing themselves into "Beijing school" and "Shanghai school," seeking small livelihoods. It truly makes one "suddenly look back and shed tears, grieving that there are no women on the high hill!" It is a pity that in the past seven or eight years, many young people who could write have either abandoned themselves to despair and become monsters, or have disappeared due to special reasons, and are now all silent. This is the fault of the environment and must be specially assigned to the heads of "scholars," "officials," and "gentlemen."

Western Journey Diary (3) 189

— Yu Dafu

Entering the mountain for a mile or two, the terrain gradually rises. The mountain path is winding and tortuous, following a stream between the two peaks. On one side is a clear stream, on the other is a sheer cliff. Where the cliff is steep, halfway up the mountain, the four characters "Linglong Wonderland" are engraved. Further up is Dongpo's Drunken Sleeping Stone and the Nine-Bend Cliff. The ruins of the Three-Rest Pavilion are probably also in this Niushan Mountain. The number of cliff carvings is countless. It is a pity that this mountain is all sandy rock, and the weathering is severe, so most of the stone carvings are no longer recognizable. The most wonderful thing is Su Dongpo's Drunken Sleeping Stone, on the west side of the mountain stream, on the east side of the road under the stone wall, a long square stone, lying horizontally, can accommodate the length of one person's body, truly like a stone sofa. Whether Dongpo actually slept drunk on this stone or not, let's not worry about it, but the three characters on the stone, and the three characters "Nine-Bend Cliff" on the rock wall not far from this stone, as well as the poem "When did two ancient dragons stand stiffly?", are said to be Dongpo's writing; I am not an archeological epigrapher, I privately think that it is better to pretend to recognize these ancient sites as genuine, and to fake elegance is ultimately more interesting than burning the zither to cook a crane. Also, to the east of the Drunken Sleeping Stone, there is also a rock, standing horizontally by the stream, with the two seal characters "Appreciating Zither Sound" engraved on it, presumably because the flowing water makes a zither-like sound, a clever double entendre with the Zither Cao Tomb just above it, and because I cannot bear to bury the author's painstaking effort, I mention it here.

Following the stream and touching the wall, ascending another fifty or sixty steps, passing the Hejian Spring, to a flat area below the top of the mountain, there is a road that winds south to the foot of a branch peak on the west side. Following the road south, to a protruding flat area, probably the old site of the Shoujuan Pavilion. Sitting here and looking south, the mountains and fields far and near are within sight, and the open space can accommodate three or four hundred people. On the north side of the open space, where the mountain peak has been cut away, a stone overhang remains, covering three ancient stone carvings below, said to be the posthumous portraits of Dongpo, Buddha Seal, and Shangu, probably the place where Chu Dong of the Ming dynasty said he obtained the portraits in a dream and built a monument for them, and also the site of the remaining pavilion recorded by Huang Dingxiang of the Ming dynasty, all in this area. It is commonly mistaken for the Three-Rest Pavilion, even mistakenly as the Three-Sage Shrine, undoubtedly all misunderstandings.

Gazing from under the stone overhang for a long time, I still followed the original road north and east, passing a monument pavilion in a vegetable garden, and went to the Linglong Mountain Temple to rest. After sitting for a while and drinking a bowl of tea, I followed the old monk to the top of the east peak, and after passing the bell tower, I arrived at Zither Cao's tomb. A desolate mound of earth, a rough stone tablet, with only the three large characters "Zither Cao's Tomb" engraved on it. Flipping through the new and old Lin'an County Chronicles, there is no record of Zither Cao's deeds, but it says that the tomb is east of the temple, only Feng Mengzhen's poem "Zither Cao's Tomb":

The strings are silent, wet with dew, in the depths of white clouds, a cold kasaya, where are the golden bones of the three springs, a night of west wind sweeps away the fallen flowers. I copy it here, to cover the shame of the compilers of the Lin'an County Chronicle.

Fellow traveler Pan Guangdan is a researcher of Feng Xiaoqing, and Lin Yutang is a passionate lover of Li Xiangjun in the Peach Blossom Fan. When everyone arrived at Zither Cao's tomb, they all became indignant and said that the compilers of the Lin'an County Chronicle were completely ignorant. Yutang even concocted a story from "A Rustic's Idle Talk", and said with impassioned words:

"Guangdan, you go and repair Feng Xiaoqing's tomb, I intend to repair Li Xiangjun's tomb, this Zither Cao's tomb, you can only let you repair it."

As he spoke, his eyes were fixed on us, the so-called you referring to us. Because of this piece of nonsense, I wrote four lines of doggerel:

The mountain is exquisite, the water is clear, Dongpo once visited Yunying here, why do the eight volumes of the Lin'an Chronicle not record a segment of Zither Cao's feelings.

On Looking at Cockroach-like People with Contempt 190

— Lin Yutang

Brother Lie Wen:

Mr. Ye Rong sighs that the world is what it is, but I am sighing about who is in the world? If there were only people like Ye Rong in the world, then there would only be great articles. In a prosperous age, they would yield in the royal court and sing praises of the sage's virtue. In a chaotic world, they would only be filled with impassioned sighs. There would inevitably be those who are good at using the nation, either relatively silent, or loudly shouting, or initiating kneeling petitions demanding unpaid wages, or organizing destruction groups to demonstrate against weak women. I can grow old and die without interacting with such people. But such people have existed since ancient times, there is nothing to be surprised about. The Analects has long been despised by such people, and the world will inevitably be looked at with contempt by such people, it is all within expectations. Because Mr. Jin Rong writes in vernacular, he deeply hates the airs of the literati and is no different from the literati who opposed vernacular and maintained traditional orthodoxy in the past. Mr. Jin Rong values "the universe" and despises "cockroaches", but I despise the universe and like to talk about cockroaches. If you ask what is there to talk about cockroaches, please read the first issue of "The World of People", "Jin Shengtan's Extreme Micro-Essays". People who do not understand this article will definitely look at cockroaches with contempt. There are many such people in the world. So Mr. Jin Rong's article says "Now I only see a few cockroaches", as if a few words are enough to devalue the worth of the "World of People". However, I know that cockroaches will not stop entering essays because of the contempt of Mr. Jin Rong. Essays will not lessen its charm because of the contempt of Mr. Jin Rong. Mr. Jin Rong can open his eyes wide to see it. What Mr. Jin Rong likes to talk about is the world and people's hearts, but if the world and people's hearts are not started from the micro details. They are often talked about until dizzy and do not know what they are talking about. Reading it, it has quite a bit of ups and downs, but when a microscope is used, it makes people laugh. If my brother does not believe, there is the following article as proof. Mr. Jin Rong said that although Zhou Zuoren is good at writing essays, he has not been able to write novels. Lu Xun did not write essays before he wrote excellent novels, hoping to prove that my saying "the creation of excellent novels comes from the training of essays" is wrong. What follows is a new stereotype:

"If you say that there is another reason, that is to exaggerate and steal the name of the essay. If you say that it is true, that is the publisher is acting against his heart and deceiving the world."

Although the two words "if" are used quite vigorously, the two assumptions are both related or contradictory, I am afraid that the author is not very clear, but he wants to use this to be able to match "acting against his heart and deceiving the world" with "exaggerating and stealing the name". It can be seen that if people do not start from the small and micro places, the world and people's hearts will often be unable to talk through.

Mr. Jin Rong said that "personal infatuation with playing things, sketching lightly, this is the essay". This is very representative of the new moralistic viewpoint. Is this not much different from the general literati's views that previously advocated "essays" and now oppose "essays" one after another?

Obsession 191

— Zang Kejia

The intersection was full of people, as if surrounding something, everyone formed a circle, tiptoeing and craning their necks, looking forward.

"What are they looking forward to?"

I also inserted my head into a gap. There was nothing strange, an old woman beggar was feeding two dogs. It wasn't strange, but it was a little strange. Everyone said that beggars are stingy, otherwise, why would they pick out all the better parts of the hard-earned food to feed these two animals, while they only eat the leftovers, making the dogs as fat as clay figures while the person is thinner than dry firewood. Some women whispered that the old beggar must owe these two dogs in her previous life.

The real situation is really difficult to make people look at it normally. The old woman was wearing a body of rags, one piece hanging over another. Her face was haggard, and she kept chewing food and sending it to the mouths of the two dogs, while constantly muttering, this mutter was like a kind of comfort. The two dogs, one white and one black, had glossy fur, each with a red ribbon tied around its neck, their heads turned up towards her, constantly wagging their tails, and humming a kind of sound in their mouths, like love. Finally, the old woman left, with the two dogs following her, one on each side.

I often think that life is nothing else, it is "obsession", "obsession" is the quality of life! What you are "obsessed" with may seem unworthy to others, then you should not care about these things. Only when you reach the point of "not being discouraged even if the whole world disapproves" can you be considered truly "obsessed". Perhaps "obsession" to the extreme is "greatness". "Obsession" is "singleness of thought" as if Marx said that the only way to his success was "singleness of thought".

This old woman beggar can also be said to be "obsessed" with these two dogs, right?

Spring Outing 192

Ghosts of the Past 193

— Hu Feng

Among those who were once "literary youths" ten years ago, there are probably some who still remember the blind poet Eroshinko. Although he shouted that our country was a "desert" after drifting from Japan, after all, after a storm of the "May Fourth Movement," many young people were dreaming while looking at the blue sky, creating smiles in their troubles, so his "Peach-Colored Clouds" and "Fairy Tales" were embraced by our pure hearts, increasing the courage that was indispensable to those who were groping in the dark.

But there is another thing that I often remember with a different feeling, which is his lecture called "Ghosts of the Past". The content was translated by Mr. Zhou Zuoren, who was standing at the forefront of the new literary movement at the time, saying that in you (the Chinese youths at the time) there are still many "ghosts of the past" living, who will run out from time to time, and encourage you to do things according to their wishes. This is very simple, but when said by him in that poetic way, it was simply vivid and captured us, making us even look back warily when we were walking on the road. Why did he give such a lecture that made us young people feel a little eerie? Of course, the reason cannot be known exactly, but now thinking about it, it is nothing more than that although he was blind and could not see, the dark force accumulated by this ancient country for thousands of years pressed on him with a gloomy breath, making him feel like he was about to suffocate, so he had to shout to the young people whose faces were slightly showing a new rosiness.

Time has passed, and the fighting youth of today have tempered steel and sensitivity from purity, and Eroshinko has gradually been forgotten. This is as it should be.

However, today I bought a newly published "The World of People" at a bookstall. Before reading the "delightful article" about "the greatness of the universe and the insignificance of cockroaches," I was attracted by the large photograph of Mr. Zhou Zuoren in front and his fiftieth birthday poem. Mr. Zhou made not small efforts in the "May Fourth" literary movement and in introducing foreign literature. When he turned fifty, we might still be willing to take a look at his photo, but what made me speechless were those two poems (not to mention those poems in response). If they were discovered in a collection of "Complete Library of the Four Treasuries", of course, we would slap the table and exclaim at such a "perfected" seven-character regulated verse. However, this author is the author of "Little River" who once fought for the liberation of poetry, and now the author who "talks about foxes and ghosts" and "listens to talk about ghosts all day long in the streets," but enthusiastically translated "Ghosts of the Past" for us back then. Beating Spring, Folk Song from Beijiang 194

— Zhang Mingchun

Beating spring,

Barefoot running,

Picking wild vegetables,

Pulling thatch;

Only hate that you can't run far in the fields,

The head-chopping (note 1) riot is like a wild dog,

Even if you are well-behaved,

They dare to pull you over;

Don't know what is being chewed (note 2) in the mouth

Can't not listen, but listening makes the face red

Just have to secretly be downwind,

Listening to the fine chopping murmur.

(Note 1) A term for scolding men

(Note 2) That is, the meaning of speaking

That Woman (3) 195

— Wang Yue

But life refuses to let anyone off easily. Moreover, life itself is a kind of strength and wisdom. Like the small grass under the rock, the small grass of life also stubbornly and cleverly finds its way to survive under the rock of the present society. With sores, she began to parade through this city. Shaking a small tin can, emitting mournful sounds to beg. In front of the foreign devils, she raised her hand to salute, speaking foreign pidgin. She courted the waiters in the packed-lunch shops for food. She once mingled with the crowd of refugees, falsely claiming that she was an escapee from the disaster area, and entered the relief center. But there was nothing but beatings, scoldings, and lack of freedom, and no relief. Perhaps it was because of this that she soon ran away again like a prisoner escaping from prison.

What followed was still aimless wandering, begging between the streets and the tram stations, providing materials to illustrate the nature of our existing civilization. Moving from the main street to this remote residential area was something that happened later. Those living here were traveling salesmen and small workers from companies, unemployed clerks, and barbers. Life was meager and monotonous, with only a little vitality on Sundays and at dusk. People drank cheap wine, set up square tables in the alleys to play mahjong, and strummed the erhu. Hiring servants was an extravagant fantasy in their lives; they didn't even have a doorman guarding the alley. But labor without a price, or labor with a low price, is rarely refused.

As wages, they only gave a little leftover cold rice and dishes that had already gone bad. To her, this was already very satisfying. Because it was no more suitable for a person's appetite than begging, and because of the fixed supply from many families, she was no longer starving. Moreover, she would occasionally have leftovers to satisfy her sympathy for other suffering people, or save them up, and when she was bored, like people eating snacks, she would take them out to pass the time. Because all the work was concentrated in the morning and at noon, and the alley was not wide, such boring time was common. But more often, she was either lazily sweeping the alley that didn't need to be swept again, or dragging the bamboo broom, pacing back and forth on the cement floor, letting the tattered men's leather shoes make a lonely tune.

Our Country's Representatives for the Far Eastern Games' Track and Field All-Around Events Selected: Liu Changchun and 25 Others. Selection Committee Decides on Five Methods. 196

The track and field and all-around sports selection committee for participating in this year's Far Eastern Games held a meeting yesterday morning to discuss the selection guidelines and review the results of the preliminary competition. After careful discussion, the following five methods were decided: Members present: Ma John (Chairman), Rong Qizhao, Jin Zhaojun.

(1) The first place in each event of the preliminary competition will be selected as an official representative.

(2) Those who have excellent past achievements but are unable to participate in the preliminary competition due to special circumstances will be given another opportunity for testing and verification.

(3) The second place in each event of the preliminary competition, whose results are superior and who have excellent past records, will be selected after careful consideration.

(4) Gu Huo, Wang Shilin, Ge Ke, and Liu Mingru, the second place in the high jump event of the preliminary competition, will be re-tested at a later date, and the decision on whether to accept them will be made based on their performance.

Second War for the Far Eastern Basketball Preliminary Round 197

Shanghai Defeats Nanjing with Wonderful Performance 198

Result: 33 to 21 丨 Shanghai Team Completely Regains Old Formidable State 丨 Nanjing Team Has Admirable Skills but Lacks Experience 丨 Hubei vs. Nanjing Tonight at 8 PM 199

In the second battle of the National Basketball Preliminary Round last night, Shanghai defeated Nanjing with the most beautiful and clear passing, by a score of 33 to 21. Shanghai's five tigers were able to maintain their original state, fully demonstrating their respective strengths, being brave and vigorous, but without any animosity. The entire team played as one, forcing the tenacious Nanjing team to admit defeat. Looking at Shanghai's performance last night, why did they not beat Hubei the night before? Taking things lightly and taking the lead, it was a pity. Tonight, Hubei will face Nanjing, and Hubei will likely win.

Shanghai Team Returns to Original State 200

Chen Xianglong Scored 20 Points in the Game Against Hubei 201

Yesterday, He Was Paid Special Attention to by the Opponent 202

And Relied on Management 208

The Nanjing team lacks talents like Lu Zhongen. Individual skills are still admirable, but they lack training and experience.

Chaos in Nanjing Team in the Second Half 209

The situation in the first half was

very tense, with the score fluctuating back and forth, making it difficult to tell who would win. Shanghai's lead was only five points at most. At the end of the first half, they only led by 13 to 11, a difference of only two points. In the second half, Lu Zhongen went forward to help the battle, and Chen Xianglong was like a fierce tiger out of its cage, each making contributions. As a result, Nanjing's formation was chaotic and could not recover. The largest difference in the score was 29 to 27. The Nanjing team was trapped in tight defense and had no opportunity. In terms of coordination, they were not as good as the Shanghai team.

Shanghai Takes the Lead by Two Points 210

After initial contact,

Shanghai frequently committed fouls, so Nanjing opened the scoring with free throws. After a long struggle, Qian Jingyong scored a free throw, leading 3 to 2. Sun Baoqing continued to contribute, and Qian Jingyong added two more points, making it 7 to 2, putting Nanjing at a disadvantage. Trying to improve, Zhang Changqing and Liu Mengjiu caught up with three points. Relying on Qian's efforts, Shanghai soon made it 9 to 4. Nanjing gradually expanded its offensive and showed promise, making it 9 to 9, and then 11 to 11. Both sides were poor at long-range shooting, also because the light was dazzling. Both sides fought fiercely. Lu Zhongen's goal created a 13 to 11 victory.

Nanjing Utterly Helpless 211

In the second half, the Shanghai team

Had smooth sailing, were consistently successful, and if there was no opportunity, they resolutely did not seek petty advantages. They relied on coordination and clever tactics, achieving unexpected victories. Their score soared, while the City of Nanjing suffered losses. In an instant, the score became 23 to 13, a difference of ten points. Nanjing changed their formation, but there was still no improvement. Chen Xianglong broke free of his constraints and scored three times in a row, making it 29 to 17, and then 31 to 19. At this point, the Shanghai team fully displayed their strengths, maximizing their coordination. In the end, Shanghai won with a score of 33 to 21. Referees were Zhang Guoxun and Jin Zhaojun.

After Failure of Pseudo-Organization Participation, Japan Decides to Participate in Far Eastern Games - Recognizing that Sports Diplomacy Situation Worsens After Withdrawal 225

Proposes Amendment of Charter when the Games are Held in the Philippines

Pseudo-Organization's Ambition to Participate in the Next Far Eastern Games Undimmed

(China United Press, Tokyo, 15th) After the Japanese Athletic Association received a reply from the Philippine Athletic Association last night, it convened a full meeting of its executives at the Chuo-Tei in the Marunouchi district at 9 PM, attended by 41 people. The meeting did not adjourn until 1:30 AM today. During the meeting, there were many who advocated a hard-line stance. Advisor Sugimura Yotaro repeatedly explained the advantages and disadvantages of withdrawing from the Far Eastern Games in relation to diplomacy, which led the atmosphere of the entire meeting and resulted in a decision to attend the Far Eastern Games. At 3 AM, two telegrams were sent, one to the Philippine Athletic Association and the other to the Manchurian Athletic Association. The telegram to the Philippines briefly stated, "The issue of the pseudo-Manchurian participation has ended in failure, but it is regrettable for the sake of harmony among Asian nations. We propose that the representatives of the three countries gather in Manila during the Games to amend the Far Eastern Games charter." The intention is still to allow pseudo-Manchuria to participate in the next Games.

Process of Deciding to Participate 226

(Japanese United Press, Tokyo, 15th) The plenary meeting of the Japanese Athletic Association, which had to decide on its final attitude regarding participation in the Far Eastern Games, convened yesterday at 8:30 PM at the Chuo-Tei in Marunouchi, with heated discussions and repeated twists. Honorary President Kano also attended the meeting at 10:30 PM. Other influential figures such as Vice President Hiranuma, Honorary Director Go, and Advisor Sugimura were all actively involved. As a result, the argument for participating in the Far Eastern Games gradually gained strength. At midnight on the 15th, a unanimous decision was made to participate in the 10th Far Eastern Games, while also addressing the issue of reforming the association. At 2:00 AM on the 15th, a response document to the Philippines was released, and the meeting adjourned. With this, the so-called sports diplomacy issue gradually escaped the crisis and came to a conclusion.

Reply Telegram to the Philippines 227

(Japanese United Press, Tokyo, 15th) The Japanese Athletic Association sent the following reply to the Philippine Athletic Association: "We have received your telegram of April 14 and understood all the details. The Greater Japan Athletic Association has worked with your association over the years on the Far Eastern Games with the sole intention of promoting the spirit of sports in the Far East and enhancing the friendship among the youth of Asian nations. Therefore, the Association has always strived to handle various issues related to the Games with a clear and loving spirit. Regarding the issue of the pseudo-organization athletic association participating in the Far Eastern Games, we have also disclosed our sincerity to the authorities based on this spirit. However, we regret that our true intentions have not been fully understood. Nevertheless, our Association fully understands the difficult position of the Philippines on this issue and expresses our deep sympathy. In particular, we appreciate the statement in your telegram that your association only seeks to promote the sportsmanship and friendship of all countries in the Far East. We respectfully express our appreciation for this. Therefore, our Association has decided to approach the Far Eastern Games with the above attitude in order to respond to your trust and friendship. We will explain the participation issue of the pseudo-organization athletic association based on your sincerity and propose a resolution at the General Assembly regarding the constitution issue. We are now pleased to decide to participate in this Games, which your association has advocated, and we are deeply gratified. When we feel Japan's responsibility for the pseudo-organization is significant, we will be patient and discreet and seek a solution in good faith. Respectfully, we hope for your understanding."

Statement by the Japanese Athletic Association 228

(Japanese United Press, Tokyo, 15th) The Japanese Athletic Association issued a statement under the name of Vice President Hiranuma, the gist of which is as follows:

The Greater Japan Athletic Association's strong advocacy for the participation of the pseudo-organization in the Far Eastern Games is entirely based on the essence of sports and the spirit of the Far Eastern Games. It is simply impossible to refuse participation to those who possess the actual ability to participate in the competition and who desire to do so themselves. To gladly allow them to participate is a fair and just action, which is a natural course of events in the spirit of sports. However, the process and outcome of this meeting have been constrained by the imperfect existing constitution, resulting in fruitless discussions and even despair, which is deeply regrettable. Now, according to the telegram from the Philippine Athletic Association, the organizer of the 10th Far Eastern Games, it is stated that they are abandoning all political considerations. Its spirit and purpose are not contrary to the attitude and position of this Association; only its method of argument is slightly different. This Association feels that it is necessary to reciprocate its trust and goodwill and to fulfill the aspirations of the pseudo-organization athletic association. This Association should maintain its position as a pillar of the Games and strive to persuade the neighboring associations as much as possible. Furthermore, we feel obligated to express friendship and courtesy to the two new allies, Annam and the Dutch East Indies, who are joining this Games. Therefore, this statement is to declare that we will participate in the sports Games held in Manila as usual.

China Education Federation Organizes Secondary School Spring Sports Meet Announces Sports Rules and Participation Guidelines Registration to Begin May 1 240

The Spring Sports Meet for Secondary School Students, organized by the Shanghai Secondary School Teachers' Federation, held its first preparatory committee meeting of the Competition Department yesterday. Those present were Shao Rugan, Qu Yue, Hu Zongfan, Wang Huaiying, Huang Shengbai, Jiang Xiangqing, Chen Zize, Wang Huaiqi, Wang Zhuangfei, Xiang Xianggao, Zhang Longhai, Lin Zhongke, Xu Zexiang, Zhu Youhuan, Chen Jicheng, etc. Chairman was Shao Rugan, Recorder was Xu Zexiang. They discussed and amended several proposals such as the Spring Sports Meet Regulations and Participation Guidelines. The sports regulations and participation guidelines are recorded below:

Sports Regulations 241

(1) The name of this association is the Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Teachers' Federation-Sponsored Municipal Secondary School Spring Sports Meet. (2) The purpose of this association is to promote sports in secondary schools in this city. (3) All public and private secondary schools in this city may request to join this association, but sports schools or sports departments are only allowed to participate in performances. (4) The venue for this association is the China Athletic Field on Labor Father Road. (5) The dates of this association are May 17, 18, and 19, starting at 1 PM each day. (6) This association shall have one honorary president, two honorary vice presidents, one president, one vice president, and one director-general to preside over all affairs. It shall also be divided into two departments: administrative and competitive, each with one director. The administrative department shall be divided into six sections: general affairs, accounting, documentation, editing, reception, and discipline. The competitive department shall be divided into two sections: competition and venue. The staff of each section shall be hired by this association. (7) Sports are divided into two parts: track and field events and group exercises. The items are as follows: A. Track and Field Events: (1) Men's Field Events: Long Jump, High Jump, Pole Vault, Discus, Shot Put, Javelin, Triple Jump, (2) Men's Track Events: 100 Meters, 200 Meters, 400 Meters, 800 Meters, 1,500 Meters, 110 Meter Hurdles, 800 Meter Relay, 1,600 Meter Relay, (3) Women's Field Events: High Jump, Long Jump, Javelin, Shot Put, Softball Throw, (4) Women's Track Events: 50 Meters, 100 Meters, 200 Meters, 400 Meter Relay. B. Group Exercises are divided into freehand, apparatus, games, dance, martial arts, military exercises, etc.

Grouping Standards 242

(8) Male and female track and field athletes are divided into two groups, A and B. The grouping standards are as follows: Male, Group A: 115 pounds or more, Group B: less than 115 pounds; Female, Group A: 100 pounds or more, Group B: less than 100 pounds. (9) Each track and field athlete may register for a maximum of four events for men and three events for women, excluding relays. For each event, each school may send a maximum of four athletes per group. (10) The top four finishers will be recognized in each men's and women's track and field event. (11) (1) This association's track and field championships are divided into six in total, including men's Group A and B track and field events, and women's Group A and B track and field events. (11) (2) Group exercises will not be judged for championships but will be performed. (11) (3) The judging rules will be based on the rules of the National Games. (11) (4) These regulations shall be implemented with the approval of the Secondary School Teachers' Federation.

Participation Guidelines 243

(1) Qualifications: Athletes from each school must be bona fide students of that school and shall be selected and sent by the schools. (2) Registration: Each school shall register with the preparatory office of this association for athletes participating in the competition, from May 1 to May 10. After the registration deadline, the sports items may not be changed. (3) Unit: Athletes participate in the competition as a school unit. (4) Expenses: The miscellaneous expenses required by athletes from each school shall be borne by themselves. (5) The preparatory office of this association is located on the second floor of the Shanghai Bank on Ximen, Shanghai Secondary School Teachers' Federation.

Shen Bao Medical Weekly

Tuberculosis and Socioeconomic Status (Part 1) 252

— Weng Zhilong

Tuberculosis has a close relationship with the nation and society. This disease is also called the "disease of the poor." Generally, the poorer the socioeconomic conditions of a society, the more poor people there are. The more poor people there are, the more tuberculosis there is. Why is this? Because of poor economic conditions, there is bound to be poor diet, poor living conditions, and poor mental state, making it easier for tuberculosis to occur. Poor people who get sick have no money to treat it, so they become poorer and sicker, beyond help. This is being sick because of poverty. Conversely, the more tuberculosis there is, the poorer the society's economy will be. Because there are more people with tuberculosis, they cannot work and will inevitably become unemployed. Every unemployed person in the country means one more person taking resources and one less person producing them. Under these circumstances, how can the economy of the country and society not suffer great losses? Therefore, the sicker one is, the poorer one becomes. This is being poor because of sickness. Thus, the poorer one is, the sicker one becomes, and the sicker one is, the poorer one becomes. If this cycle continues, the people will be sick, and the national strength will decline, making it easy for the nation to perish. Therefore, to save the country and cure the nation's illness, it is necessary to first cure the illness of the people. Everyone must understand that if the people are healthy, their productivity will naturally be strong. With high productivity, the economic conditions of the country and society can naturally improve. As the saying goes, "The wealth of the people is the wealth of the society and the nation." This is a natural consequence. Therefore, it can be seen that the relationship between tuberculosis and socioeconomic status is very deep. Furthermore, in our country, the number of people who die from tuberculosis each year is more than tens of thousands, and the losses to the people and the nation are more than millions of yuan. Because there are no detailed statistics, it is impossible to report an accurate percentage, which is very regrettable and very worrying. We must find a way to remedy this.

As far as I know, within five years since 1906, the losses suffered by the city of Berlin, Germany, due to the deaths of people from tuberculosis were approximately 133 trillion marks per year. Adding the loss of productivity due to death, the total loss was approximately 150 trillion marks, for a total loss of 380 trillion marks. From this, it can be seen that the losses suffered by their country in just one city due to illness were already so enormous. However, according to Moller's calculations, due to effective prevention in recent years, tuberculosis has decreased, and the country's losses have been reduced to more than one hundred trillion marks. From this, it can be seen that promoting the prevention of tuberculosis is protecting the lives and property of the people, and it is also creating wealth for the nation and maintaining its vitality. The mortality rate from tuberculosis among Chinese people is even higher than in other countries, so it can be inferred that China's property losses are even greater, making tuberculosis prevention work particularly important.

Tuberculosis is also known as tubercle bacillus disease. The cause of the disease is mostly infection with tubercle bacillus bacteria. Because of poor socioeconomic conditions, little attention is paid to prevention, and people are infected. From a medical perspective, this disease is not hereditary to descendants, but the descendants of tuberculosis patients are generally not very healthy and are easily infected or develop other diseases. This is because of weak resistance!

For example, Weiu berg's report on the mortality statistics of infants in the city of Stuttgart, Germany, from 1873 over a period of 30 years:

Out of every 100 infants, the death rate of infants whose fathers had tuberculosis was 46.82

Out of every 100 infants, the death rate of infants whose mothers had tuberculosis was 48.11

Out of every 100 infants, the death rate of infants whose fathers did not have tuberculosis was 40.27

Out of every 100 infants, the death rate of infants whose mothers did not have tuberculosis was 40.17

From this, it can be seen that the descendants of those with tuberculosis are relatively less healthy.

Common Knowledge of Skin Diseases (Part 1) 253

— Xie Yunshou

Today, I am entrusted by Dr. Wang Wanbai of the Gospel Radio Station to talk about medicine and hygiene. I do not claim to have in-depth research in medicine. If there is anything I can contribute to everyone, it is only from the aspect of skin diseases that I have learned. I will share some very basic common knowledge with everyone.

Before we talk about common knowledge of skin diseases, we must first understand a very important organ. What are its characteristics in terms of anatomy and physiology that allow it to bear such important responsibilities? I will now give a brief explanation of the anatomy of the skin.

The skin, in the eyes of ordinary people, appears to be a very thin layer. However, when a doctor cuts off a piece with an instrument and examines it under a microscope, it can be divided into three layers. The first layer is called the epidermis, the second layer is called the dermis, and the third layer is called the subcutaneous tissue. The epidermis can be roughly divided into two layers. The upper layer is called the stratum corneum, and the lower layer is called the stratum germinativum. The stratum corneum is the outermost layer of our skin, which is yellowish or white and transparent. The stratum germinativum contains a certain amount of pigment. The difference in the color of the world's races lies in the concentration of pigment in this layer. Furthermore, it is in contact with the dermis and has a lymph fluid communication with the lymph fluid of the dermis. Therefore, during inflammation, the lymphocytes in the dermis can reach the epidermis. The second layer is called the dermis. The dermis contains connective tissue cells and elastic fibers. Therefore, the elasticity of the dermis is very high. In addition, there are blood vessels, lymphatic vessels, lymphatic cavities, nerves, nerve endings, sebaceous glands, sweat glands, hair, etc. It is indeed the main part of the skin. The third layer is called the subcutaneous tissue, also called subcutaneous fat tissue. This varies in thickness depending on gender, age, race, and individual health status and is not fixed.

I have roughly explained the anatomy of the skin above. Now I will talk about the physiological functions of the skin. There are many physiological functions of the skin, such as nerve function, secretion, absorption, respiration, body temperature regulation, and protection from various external harms. I will now break them down and explain them.

First, I will talk about nerve function. The sensory nerves of the skin can be divided into four types: touch, temperature, cold, and pain. Each type of sensation has a specialized nerve ending to control it. The skin uses this nerve function to know the various conditions of the outside world and can prevent disasters. For example, by using the temperature nerve, we can know the heat of fire; by using the cold nerve, we can know the coldness of ice; by using the pain nerve, we can know the invasion of knives, swords, and other external harms; and by using the touch nerve, we can know what we are touching. However, the distribution of these four types of nerve endings is not fixed. They vary depending on the location. For example, the fingertips have more touch and pain endings, so touch and pain are also the most sensitive. If the skin did not have this nerve function, great danger could occur. For example, if one did not feel the heat when encountering fire, burns could occur.

Second, I will talk about the secretory function of the skin. The skin has sweat glands and sebaceous glands. Sweat glands can secrete sweat, and sebaceous glands can secrete oil to lubricate the skin. If there is too much or too little secretion, it will turn into various diseases, such as seborrhea, lack of sebum, and acne. The main function of sweating is to excrete excess water from the body to replace the function of the kidneys. Furthermore, because of the evaporation of water, it can reduce the temperature of the skin and blood, lowering the body temperature. Sweating more in summer uses the evaporation of sweat to take away the body's temperature. It is indeed a very important method of body temperature regulation.

Third, body temperature regulation. Eighty percent of the heat dissipated from the body is released from the skin, which uses the contraction and expansion of its blood vessels. For example, in cold weather, the skin's blood vessels contract, reducing heat dissipation, so the skin is mostly pale white in cold weather (redness and swelling from frostbite is an exception). In hot weather, the skin's blood vessels expand, increasing heat dissipation, so the skin is mostly red and flushed in hot weather. Isn't that a very clever arrangement? Moreover, the skin uses the stratum corneum, the outermost layer of its epidermis, to resist high external temperatures. You see, during the hot summer, carters run barefoot on the scorching ground. On the one hand, it can also prevent excessive heat dissipation. Patients with extensive burns who have their skin peeled off are prone to weakness due to excessive heat dissipation.

Introducing Dr. Liu Yongchun, Expert in the Production of BCG Vaccine for Tuberculosis Prevention 254

— Song Guobin

Those who speak about national affairs today often sigh that there is a lack of talent. Is there really a lack of talent? It is that there is talent but it is not known how to use it. Chu did not use Miao Ben and fled to Jin, and Yu did not use Baili Xi and entered Qin. China has talent, but other countries use it. From ancient times to the present, it is the same old story. It is regrettable. Dr. Liu Yongchun studied bacteriology in France for eight years. At the Pasteur Institute in Paris, he once returned to China, but he crossed over to other countries again due to lack of opportunities. He was hired by the Pasteur Institute in Saigon, where he was in charge of BCG vaccine production. He concentrated on his studies, devoted himself to research, and achieved great results. He is a well-known expert, but the people of his own country do not yet know him. Now, he has returned to the country temporarily to visit his beloved mother. During our conversations, my admiration deepened. My relationship with him is not only one of kinship but also one of classmates. Throughout my life, I have admired him, and he is indeed a person worthy of admiration. If we are talking about talent, he should be the first choice. Nowadays, the prevention of tuberculosis is on everyone's mind, and the production of BCG requires an expert. Therefore, I am acting on the principle of impartiality and introducing him to the people of the country. Do not let useful talent be lost in a foreign land.
