Amidst the Decline of China's Silk Industry: The Global Rayon Industry 275

— Yang Guangxu

When we recall the history of China's international trade, we immediately realize how important silk and tea were to China's foreign trade. However, this glory has long since ceased to be seen again. The tea industry declined first, and the silk industry followed. Even today, scholars are advocating for the rectification of the silk industry. Recently, the National Economic Commission has even established a Silkworm Improvement Committee to recruit female silkworm breeders in order to revive China's silk industry. It is a good thing to mend the fold after the sheep is lost, but when we look at the situation today, we feel that it may be too late. With the rapid progress of the silk industries in Italy and Japan in the forefront, and the threat of rayon in the rear, it is doubtful whether China's silk industry can have any hope of revival. The purpose of this article is, on the one hand, to describe the backwardness of China's silk industry in the international market, and on the other hand, to focus on the extreme progress of the strong rayon industry. The pressure from the world silk industry, not only China, is enough to make people fear. Please first briefly describe the world silk market in recent years.

According to estimates by the French Mssrs. Morel Journel et Cie, the world silk industry declined again from 1932 to 1933, with both output decreasing and prices weakening.

World Raw Silk Supply (Thousand Tons)

From Export 1913-14 1930-31 1931-32 1932-33 1933-34

Shanghai 5,800 4,820 2,160 2,716 2,725

Guangdong 2,780 3,310 1,550 1,620

Japan 12,120 33,595 33,020 31,100 28,800

Central Asia 435 330 145 382 5

Central Europe 4,235 5,08 3,410 3,640 3,245

Italy 1,880 890 665 668 648

Total 27,365 40,045 48,96 39,733 37,064

*The estimated amount of Italian silk does not mean that Japan's output will decrease. In fact, because there is too much silk stored in New York and Japan, Japan may lower its production.

From the above, it can be seen that the world supply of silk has gradually decreased since 1930. According to the law of supply and demand, the price of silk should have risen, but this is not the case. The reason is that rayon has gradually replaced silk. According to the same source, the silk price not only did not rise, but fell sharply. Please see the table below for the prices of various silks in Lyon. (Average) Unit: Francs Place of Origin 1929 1930 1931 1932 1933

Italy 1150 155 118 88 67

Shanghai 300 90 155 105 78

Sichuan 245 40 125 85 70

Wuxi 75 65 50 36

Japan 285 170 145 92 62

From the above, it can be seen that the decline of the world silk market has been rapid, and the average market price last year was only one-fourth of that in 1929. Due to the devaluation of the Japanese yen, the loss on the Japanese side was still small, but the silk merchants in China have been unable to supply their goods to the market for sale under this sharp drop. Then, the so-called rectification of the silk industry today, the benefits that can be obtained are probably very small. Observing from a global perspective, even if China can revive the silk industry, its position in the international market is still difficult to predict. Or to put it bluntly, today's silk is not an irreplaceable product, and the need for silk is no longer active in reality.

Tracing back to the source, we can see that the decline of the silk industry is not limited to China. The momentum of rayon is enough to make silk lose its luster. Countries that previously needed silk have either tried to increase the manufacture of rayon, or purchased rayon from other countries to replace it.

In recent years, the major rayon-producing countries in the world have actively increased their production, and the needs of the world have also prompted them to speed up production. In order to fundamentally discuss the reason for the decline of the silk industry, we cannot but review this rayon industry.

In the United Kingdom and other countries, the progress of rayon manufacturing technology has made rayon yarn sufficient in quality and practicality to be used for various textiles. At the same time, the price has become lower due to the increase in work efficiency. As a result, the need for the silk industry has been greatly affected. Even cotton and wool have been affected.

The country with the largest rayon production in the world is the United States, which has always maintained its leading position. We can obtain the production of rayon in various countries in the world, as shown in the table below. (Unit: Thousand Pounds)

Country 1933 1932 1931 1930

United States 172,105 131,085 140,800 115,000

Japan 89,925 64,395 46,750 33,330

United Kingdom 84,080 72,510 54,570 48,870

Italy 82,040 70,145 76,120 59,700

Germany 68,200 64,680 55,000 57,880

France 57,200 47,255 36,365 39,160

Netherlands 23,650 19,405 19,800 15,840

Switzerland 10,560 2,055 9,900 9,600

Belgium 9,605 9,780 10,395 10,450

Canada 7,610 7,120 5,565 4,840

Other 10,495 21,145 15,525 55

Total 625,470 518,575 470,790 410,225

From the above, it can be seen that the rayon industry is showing the opposite trend to the silk industry. The increase in production last year reached more than 100 million pounds. We seem to be unable to ignore the progress of the rayon industry.

Japan's production increased by more than 20 million pounds last year. Japan's production is competitive in the international market due to lower raw material prices and special labor costs, especially in the Far East, where rayon fabrics compete more fiercely with cotton fabrics.

The United Kingdom's production also increased by more than 10 million pounds, and most of the increase was consumed in the domestic market and did not need to be exported. Since January of last year, various manufacturing companies decided to accelerate production by 30% and reduce the price by 3 pence per pound. Moreover, after processing, there is no need to build more factories, only to improve the existing factories, so the cost has been reduced. In the United Kingdom, this is gradually becoming a force opposing cotton, but the tax rate on rayon in the United Kingdom is very high, so it is difficult to compete with cotton. The competition against silk is not affected by this, because the tax on silk is also higher.

In the United States, the production increase last year was the largest, at more than 40 million pounds. In particular, a type of acetate rayon is the most daunting, because some clothing powders can be woven from it. Although the price is higher than the general type, the consumption volume has not declined slightly. Especially at the end of last year, sales were the most prosperous, and those who made underwear had to use it.

In addition, the progress of this industry in major European countries cannot be denied. Italy and the Netherlands are trying to increase manufacturing in order to export and compete with Japan's silk industry. Moreover, the cartel system is still prevalent in Europe, seeking to standardize the price of cloth. France is also working hard to increase manufacturing in order to reduce the import of silk.

With the rise of the rayon industry in recent years, the silk industry has been greatly affected. The United States, which used to be the largest sales market, has become the leader in the rayon industry, and France, which is famous for its Lyon silk market, is also stepping up its manufacture and use of rayon. It can be seen that today's silk seems to have a sense of being left behind. However, it is not the case. People must not give up on its rectification because of this. Silk has many things that rayon cannot match. Today, the reason why rayon is full of products is because of its low price and good quality. However, it is well known that it is not durable. The price of silk is naturally higher than that of rayon, but its durability is not comparable to that of rayon. Moreover, with the economic decline of the world, the purchasing power of people in various countries has decreased, so they have abandoned the durable silk and taken the cheap and easily damaged rayon.

Moreover, in terms of the situation in China, the organization and increase of silk are secondary. The most important thing is the improvement of quality. If we can earnestly rectify the quality, on the one hand, we can compete with Japan and Italy, and on the other hand, we can gradually eliminate the arrogance of rayon. Now is the time to advocate the plan for the rectification of silk, but I hope that the people of the country can recognize the current malpractices, and then prescribe the right medicine, in order to talk about the hope of revival. May our people work hard!

Further Discussion on Fisheries Investigation and its Strategies 276

— Ruo Qian

It was reported in the newspaper the other day that the authorities are planning to unify and control the national fisheries industry.

After reading it, I felt overjoyed, and I believe that people in the fisheries industry share the same feeling. The other day, I discussed that the basis of unification and control lies in a clear understanding of the principles involved. A clear understanding of the principles requires a detailed investigation. Now, I will further discuss my limited views with people in the society.

Fisheries investigation is considered by all countries as the most important fundamental work for all fisheries facilities. Let's take Japan as an example. In 1931, Japan initiated the Economic Rehabilitation Movement for agricultural, mountainous, and fishing villages. At that time, due to the economic downturn in various areas in the preceding years, the output of products dropped abnormally. Agricultural, mountainous, and fishing villages felt especially exhausted. Therefore, the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry established the Economic Rehabilitation Department, which was divided into four sections to specialize in this matter. On the one hand, various lecture meetings were held to disseminate information about the matter. On the other hand, the Great Japan Fisheries Association and the Imperial Fisheries Association, the two major authorities in the fisheries industry, jointly conducted economic surveys of fishing villages. The significance of the survey was to accurately understand the economic and industrial situation of the fishing villages, as well as the environmental and social conditions of the area, in order to establish the direction of the economic rehabilitation plan for agricultural, mountainous, and fishing villages. Japan has always attached importance to investigation and has statistics for various places over the years. However, even at the beginning of the planning direction, a large-scale and detailed investigation is still necessary. This shows that if we want to improve and construct a career, we must start with investigation.

Now, what is the state of the fisheries industry in our country? Don't you see that the number of fishing boats is decreasing day by day? The price of fish is falling day by day? Imported aquatic products are flooding in like a tide, and sea pirates are as numerous as cattle hairs. The result of this cycle is to promote the overall bankruptcy of the fisheries industry. Therefore, since the beginning of the Republic of China, predecessors in the aquatic products industry have been running around and calling for the hope of reviving the fisheries industry. As a result, some people have established aquatic products schools, some have held new-style fishing vessels, and some have established fisheries experimental fields. Gradually, to this day, the country and society have become aware of the importance of the fisheries industry. Don't you see the publicity in newspapers and magazines? The government's plans? However, what is the state of the fisheries industry in our country? I am afraid it is still groping in the dark, which makes the publicity words easily like clouds passing by, and the implementation of the plan like building a house in the desert. That is why for more than 20 years, people have been shouting and advocating with all their might, but have not received the slightest success so far! Is this not because we have not been able to know the original situation of our country in detail? Therefore, it is believed that if we want to reorganize and develop the fisheries industry in our country, we must start with investigation.

However, everyone knows that the investigation is difficult to carry out. Fisheries investigation is no exception. Therefore, there must be a precise investigation plan before we can follow the map and achieve success. It is believed that the purpose of the fisheries investigation needed in our country today is to investigate the economic and technical conditions of the national fisheries industry, so as to compile investigation reports and serve as research and suggestions for fishery policy facilities and fishery construction. And its greatest purpose is to serve as a reference for future unification and control, in order to seek the revitalization of the entire fisheries industry. Therefore, the investigation area should cover the whole country. However, due to the vast scope of fisheries, marine fisheries should be investigated first. At the same time, important freshwater fisheries should be handled first. The scope of the investigation should cover all aspects, such as the economic conditions of labor, capital, trade, fishery village organization, and fishermen's life; the natural conditions of fishing grounds, fishery products, and fishing seasons; the technical conditions of fishing boats, fishing gear, fishing methods, aquaculture, and manufacturing. In addition, the population, culture, transportation, consumption power, labor force, and commodity prices related to various conditions cannot be omitted rashly. The strategy of investigation should be to personally investigate. Therefore, a national fisheries investigation general agency should be established to formulate an investigation plan, and then gradually proceed step by step in order to achieve great results.

So, what is the strategy for investigation? It is believed that the actual investigation of fishing villages in various places should be carried out to prepare for future measures to stabilize fishing villages and control sales. On the one hand, individual investigations should be carried out on the important production fisheries in the country (especially those with oceanic characteristics) to serve as a technique for production control. Please elaborate on it. Why do we advocate the investigation of fishing villages? Fishing villages are the birthplace of fisheries and the self-sufficient unit of the country. What we hope for in fishing villages is the paradise of fishing villages. Therefore, all residents of fishing villages must have the spirit of coexistence and co-prosperity, the technology of fishing and aquaculture, and the need to protect fishing grounds and aquatic animals. For their own operations, they must be hardworking and resilient. Then the fishing villages will be stable, and the fisheries can be revived. However, we still cannot say the strategy for the prosperity of fishing villages. Today, although the fishing villages in our country know that they are bankrupt and collapsing, it is difficult to obtain a definite conclusion on the degree of fragmentation and collapse. How can we talk about rectifying and arranging them freely? Moreover, the fishing villages themselves have their inherent difficulties. The fishermen in fishing villages and the farmers in rural areas are very different in their production. Farmers have the land rights of cultivated land and the ownership of immovable products produced on their land (although there are now many farmers who rent land for cultivation, but in theory, it is always like this, and fishermen mostly operate by borrowing). Therefore, their own labor, diligence, and technology are the key to their direct interests. Therefore, farmers' work does not harm others, nor is it harmed by others. However, fishermen are the opposite. They fish in the public waters 丨 fishing grounds 丨 to capture mobile aquatic animals. Moreover, the so-called fishermen can operate freely at any time and in any fishing ground, regardless of anyone. Therefore, if they do not catch, they will be caught by others, and early catching will harm others. Therefore, the coastal fishing grounds have become the battlefield of fishing villagers, and the diligence and technology of fishermen have only become weapons. Therefore, if we want to rationalize the operation of fishing villages and make the state of fishing villages a paradise, we must promote the spirit of mutual assistance, and take the environment of fishing villages in various places as the background, and solve conflicts according to local conditions, and then there is hope. However, in order to use the power of guidance and control to achieve the effect of fishing village prosperity, and to take measures according to local conditions, it is really useless if we do not conduct economic investigations of individual fishing villages. Now, please speak with facts. The cuttlefish fishery in Jiangsu and Zhejiang used to be captured by trawling, but now the fishermen in Wenzhou and Taizhou capture them with cuttlefish cages. However, the function of cuttlefish cages is to reduce labor and increase catches. Therefore, they think that they have made contributions to improving fishing gear and catch indiscriminately everywhere. However, the laying of cuttlefish cages is a kind of fixed fishing gear, which occupies most of the fishing ground area, causing the original fishermen to lose their production channels. Moreover, the cages are often attached with cuttlefish eggs, which must be scraped off with knives and sticks when collecting catches. Therefore, there must be many that cannot hatch, which will greatly hinder the breeding of cuttlefish. Therefore, the original fishermen are also justified in wanting to eliminate this abnormal development, and conflicts arise between fishing villages. Due to the corruption of the past fishery administration, and the failure to understand the situation, the blood case of the double gang fight on Yuanhua Mountain was caused. Therefore, if the situation of fishing villages in various places is clearly investigated, and appropriate fishery management personnel and guidance personnel are placed, they will be educated, guided, and improve the organization of fishing villages to promote the spirit of mutual assistance and mutual love. On the one hand, administrative power will be used to divide fishing areas, and technology will be tested to protect breeding and increase production. Then the fishing villages will be stable and the fisheries will be revitalized. Therefore, it is believed that the economic investigation of fishing villages is indispensable.

Why do we promote the individual investigation of important fisheries? The important fisheries are large in scale and high in production, and involve many parties, which are enough to affect the prosperity and decline of the national fisheries industry. Therefore, according to the needs of the facts, we should organize the national system of this fishery for the convenience of unified control. In terms of itself, this fishery has its common needs for technology and equipment. Therefore, organizing a group of this fishery and bringing all the operators of this fishery under unified control can unify the goals and share the benefits, so that they can plan together to seek the improvement of themselves. Moreover, important fisheries have their internal common points and external different points. Therefore, individual investigations must be carried out. And in terms of the fact of investigation, important fisheries mostly have a very wide range of fishing. If the investigation is carried out by region, and involves more than two provinces and two regions, the measures will definitely feel difficult. Moreover, the so-called important fisheries are mostly oceanic fisheries in nature. Their fishing grounds, fishing gear, and operations cannot be tied to fishing villages. Moreover, how should we nurture, maintain, and promote important fisheries so that they become formal oceanic fisheries and promote the revitalization of the entire fisheries industry? Therefore, important fisheries need individual investigation. Furthermore, the possibilities of oceanic fisheries in our country cannot go to the outer sea to fish. Most of them are transferred to coastal fishing grounds. Therefore, they must be individually controlled to promote progress. For example, the new-style steamship fisheries in our country are all transferred to the coastal fishing grounds. Therefore, since the establishment, the catches have been reduced, and the coastal fishermen have been hit. It is believed that the tragic decline of fisheries in recent years is not unrelated to this. However, steamship operators must also have their difficulties, such as insufficient capital, lack of technical personnel, and steamship operators are all business-oriented, and cannot abandon fishing work to investigate the ocean and explore fishing grounds. Therefore, we should first know the current situation, investigate in detail, and promote the formation of this industry group. The highest fishery control agency will directly control it and provide various assistance in terms of technology (the establishment of instructors, the holding of investigation ships) and economy (low-interest loans, the establishment of bonuses). Then the establishment of oceanic fisheries is promising, and the revitalization of the entire fisheries industry is also promising. Therefore, it is considered that if we want to reorganize and develop fisheries, the investigation of the economic situation of important fisheries is indispensable.

As for the strategy of investigation, the establishment of a national fisheries research institute is the most important thing. Then the general institute and the provinces and cities should jointly form branch institutes. Then the general institute will conduct individual investigations of important fisheries, and the branch institutes will conduct investigations of fishing villages. The results of the two investigations will be compiled into statistical reports and sent to the general institute for research, and then published to the society for common discussion. Now, I will draft an outline of the organization based on my limited views, and offer it for discussion and correction.

1. Establish a national fisheries research institute with three departments: general affairs, investigation, and publication. Then, jointly establish investigation branch institutes with provinces and cities, which also have three departments: general affairs, investigation, and publication. However, under the general institute, there is also a research committee, which is divided into four departments: fishing village organization, fishery economy, fishery technology, and compilation. There is also a training committee, which is divided into technical training classes, fishing village education classes, and warehouse management classes (regarding the management of fish markets and aquatic products warehouses).

2. Tasks: The national fisheries research institute is tasked with investigating the situation of national fisheries. The general affairs department is responsible for (1) matters related to official documents and all documents; (2) matters related to the budget and final accounts of all expenses in the institute. The investigation department is responsible for (1) thorough investigation of certain fisheries; (2) investigation and statistics of various fisheries; (3) guiding and training national fishery situation correspondents to establish an accurate investigation foundation; (4) joint investigation with national aquatic products schools and testing agencies. The publication department is responsible for (1) reporting on the results of investigation and statistics; (2) research reports on certain issues; (3) translating and publishing research reports and other related items on the aquatic products industry in various countries. The research committee is to research the results of the national fisheries investigation and to propose a national fisheries design. Therefore, the fishing village organization department is responsible for (1) matters related to the public security and education of fishing villages; (2) matters related to various aquatic products organizations. The fishery economy department is responsible for (1) reducing production costs; (2) stabilizing finance; (3) facilitating transportation and sales; (4) controlling trade. The fishery technology department is responsible for (1) fishing technology; (2) aquaculture technology; (3) manufacturing technology. The compilation department is responsible for compiling and translating academic investigations and research reports on the aquatic products industry in various countries. The task of the investigation branch institute is to investigate the various aspects of the fisheries industry in the area. Therefore, the lowest responsibility of the investigation department is (1) investigation of important fishery production areas; (2) investigation of important fishery consumption areas; (3) economic investigation of fishing villages; (4) investigation of trade; (5) technical investigation of manufacturing and aquaculture; (6) economic investigation of labor and transportation. In addition, due to the length of the article, the investigation methods and various items are not listed in detail. The organization system of the investigation institute is listed below to end this article, and I hope that experts from all over the world will correct it.

Securities: Affected by the North China Situation, the Bond Market Fluctuated Wildly Last Week 278

Last week, from April 9 to April 14, the Chinese Securities Exchange's public bond market underwent sudden changes after a four-day Spring Festival holiday. The North China situation became thorny due to the Japanese demand for postal and traffic connections. Huang Fu left Ping to go to Gan, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense. The market sentiment was quite panicked. There were many short positions in the market, and the North Gang even sold wildly. The situation on Monday was therefore extremely bad. The entire day declined, with a sharp drop of several jiao to more than three yuan in one day, which was a rare change in recent months. On Tuesday, as the atmosphere eased, various gangs rushed to cover their positions, and retail investors were especially eager to buy. In one day, the three sessions rebounded by several jiao to 1.78 yuan. On Wednesday, the upward trend continued, with No. 75 covering more positions, continuing to improve by 23 jiao to 1 yuan. On Thursday and Friday, the news was dull, Huang Fu still failed to return to Ping, and various parties had different opinions. The North Gang gradually covered their positions, and market prices still rose and fell unevenly, high and low, with a small number. On Saturday, the news of traffic and postal connections seemed to have been resolved, and the atmosphere suddenly eased. A giant household turned from short to long, and the market suddenly became good. No. 11 gradually covered their positions, and market prices rebounded throughout the day, improving by 34 jiao to 1 yuan. As a result of the week's market prices, the gains and losses were mixed, about 23 jiao. The trend has gradually recovered the number that fell on Monday. The total turnover was 116,468,000 yuan. Piece Goods: Different Views on the Sales of Flannel 282

Flannel sales have increased by one-third in recent years because women choose it as a coat material. However, although women's flannel has a high profit margin, it easily falls out of fashion, so few manufacturers make it. Most of them deal in men's flannel. Currently, both types of flannel are selling well both locally and in other cities, but their sales patterns are different. Sichuan, Tianjin, Beiping, Hankou, Qingdao, and other places mostly sell high-end goods above six yuan, with no inquiries for women's flannel. In Jingjiang, Suzhou, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Wuhu, Hangzhou, Ningbo, and other places, mostly low-end goods below four yuan are sold. Except for large-scale orders in the capital, women's flannel is rarely touched.

Recent Inquiries for Chinese and Foreign Silk and Satin 283

"Domestic Silk and Satin" Since the Meiya Factory stopped production, small factories have increased their production. Due to the sluggishness of the current silk market, no panic has been seen yet. Regarding the Sichuan Gang, two hundred odd pieces of silk plain silk were loaded yesterday, with a selling price of one yuan and five cents per yard, being a high-quality fabric. There were also some transactions for fancy Tian silk and Power Loom Fabric, totaling fifty odd pieces, with a selling price of one yuan and one dime per measure. The Beiping, Tianjin, and Hankou Gangs only slightly purchased. Transactions for thin goods on this street are still fragmented, and prices are still fair.

"Foreign Silk and Satin" Since last month, new goods have continuously arrived, but the quantity is still small. As usual, the scarcity makes the goods expensive, so market prices are trending firm and high. Erqi Shi Rui Tai plain cloth, four yuan and one dime and five cents per yard (increased by two dimes compared to the old price); Sanshi Yi Shi Hua Jia plain cotton cloth, five yuan and eight dimes and five cents per yard (increased by three dimes compared to the old price); Erqi Shi Tian Feng fancy cotton cloth, five yuan and four dimes and five cents per yard (increased by two dimes). Fancy plain silk velvet and Quan silk also continue to arrive, and prices are also firm. Many people are coming to purchase, mostly selling directly to the market by silk and satin shops.

Oil Market: White Tung Oil is Becoming Increasingly Weak 284

Since white tung oil was sold by foreign firms in Hankou for twenty-seven yuan and six dimes, the market has gradually shown signs of weakness. For several days, foreign firms have not discussed transactions, so the situation is trending towards softening. Although there are currently no transactions, the opening price will likely not be a large drop. The opening price of cargo by Hankou firms has already fallen to slightly above twenty-one yuan, while the price for Zhi Tong oil is around twenty-one yuan. Zhejiang Tung oil initially echoed the Hankou market, once exceeding twenty-two yuan per dan in river transactions, but has now also fallen to around twenty-one yuan. In short, after the market reaches a peak, a decline is naturally possible. Furthermore, foreign firms in Hankou repeatedly suspend purchases after seeing the market rise. Since domestic sales cannot be stimulated, everything relies on foreign sales as the main body, so the rise and fall of the market entirely depends on the presence or absence of foreign sales. Local firms in this port mainly rely on domestic sales, so they are not very interested in this price surge and still respond with a silent attitude. Very few are currently purchasing. Now that they see prices falling, it seems to have been anticipated. After all, spring sales were too dismal, so even a rise and fall is not enough to stimulate interest.

Supplement to the Shanghai Edition of Shen Bao

Talking Points

Gandhi's Victory 285

— Huan Sheng

Mahatma Gandhi, who advocated non-cooperation to seek the independence and liberation of the Indian nation, advised his countrymen on the seventh of this month: "For the sake of freedom, temporarily suspend civil resistance." As soon as this advice was issued, the British considered that "Gandhi's move will greatly affect the national situation, and it is felt that there should be some kind of reciprocal gesture. Therefore, non-cooperative political prisoners will be gradually released...The legislative bill on the Prevention of Disorder Ordinance may not be cancelled for a while, but it will be shelved...The order prohibiting the National Congress will also be revoked, and the headquarters of the National Congress and the provincial branches will be allowed to reopen meetings," and so on.

This Gandhi, who is known as the leader of the Indian national movement, has been seeking independence and liberation by advocating economic non-cooperation with his thin and bony figure for many years. He has been imprisoned many times and even resorted to starvation, but he has not been able to obtain any results in the so-called National Conference and Round Table Conference. Now, he has surprisingly obtained the grace and pardon of the British Empire with a small piece of advice, which cannot be regarded as an unprecedented victory in his efforts to promote the national movement.

However, because of this victory, and thinking about the future of the 300 million Indian people, we don't know whether to laugh or cry. Because the ultimate goal of the modern imperialist powers' aggression against weak national colonies is, of course, economic plunder, but maintaining this economic exploitation requires a powerful political, naval, and air military force. If the form of national revolutionary war is not used to crush it, the so-called liberation and independence is nothing more than a dream during deep sleep. This understanding has already made us question what path Gandhi's so-called economic non-cooperation will lead Indian national liberation to. What's more, now that "civil resistance has been temporarily suspended for the sake of freedom," even this point has been abandoned.

In India, where British economic power completely dominates the entire social life, advocating economic non-cooperation, if it can be realized, is tantamount to 300 million Indian people sacrificing for "non-cooperation," starving to death, or else it is a self-deceiving fantasy in the name of liberation and independence for a part of the people. Perhaps it is because India is "a sacred land of purity and inaction, which does not value force," so that non-cooperation can still secretly breed and rise there, but in essence, it is a comical fact of strangling one's own throat and letting others slaughter. Therefore, no matter what Gandhi's noble ideals are in his mind, objectively he is an obstacle to the independence and liberation of the Indian nation in any case. In the sense of blinding the people's minds, diverting them from political struggles and limiting them to passive, non-cooperative actions, in the sense of weakening the people's courage and only relying on economic exclusion without seeking armed resistance, it is more accurate to say that Gandhi is the culprit of this movement than to say that he is the leader of Indian national independence and liberation.

Now Gandhi is changing again and again, from non-cooperation to "temporarily suspending civil resistance," so that the goal that the British could not achieve by enticing participation in the Round Table Conference with preferential treatment in prison has been realized all of a sudden. How can this not make the hardworking British "express their joy"? Especially after the armed disturbances in northern India not long ago, it is natural that this trend cannot be allowed to rise, and there is much reliance on this old man. This is why the British "bestow imperial grace," and Gandhi has achieved the victory of non-cooperation.

The British call Gandhi's advice "the new doctrine of non-resistance." Of course, the old ones will celebrate upon hearing it, "Our doctrine is not isolated." But judging from the merits of the new ones, one can't help but feel "ungrateful."

Bored People 286

— Yan Zi

How exciting should an exceptional Saturday afternoon be for me, who is spinning in the vortex of life every day? Everyone is looking forward to the arrival of this day, and I have thought so too, when I am working. Wouldn't it be great if I could spend every day like Saturday? I can sit all day, doing nothing, and be a happy person. Saturday finally came as I hoped, but my restless heart is hoping it will pass quickly, and tomorrow will be better, for it is Sunday. I can't rest, I have to work like a horse, every day, every hour, so that I have no time to think about the past, and the past cannot be replayed in my mind. But Saturday has come, this is a day of rest. After lunch, I sat leisurely on the sofa smoking, rejecting every invitation from my colleagues, staring at the ceiling in a daze. One cigarette after another, can I sit like this for a day? Finally, I asked myself, and stood up and walked out as if I was going to do something. Outside the door is a lively road, people are crowded in trams, in cars, and walking people, shoulder to shoulder, everyone has something to do. And me? I walked past a friend's house and knocked on the door as if I was going to visit him on purpose. I ran up the stairs and pushed open the small room. My friend was lying on the bed reading a book alone. He got up and said, "You came just in time, I'm bored to death!" He yawned lazily. I couldn't help but laugh secretly. There are people who are as bored as I am on Saturday. I walked to his bedside, and the closed book was a copy of Seven Heroes and Five Gallants. We looked at each other and burst out laughing.

"Little Hero Ai Hu, superb martial arts?" I said.

"I don't even know what kind of book this is. I just grabbed it and looked at it. I didn't actually see anything. Where did you come from?"

"Just as bored, so I came to see you."

"Let's go for a walk outside." He didn't ask for my consent, put on his felt hat and walked out without looking back. I seemed to think this move was very reasonable and closed the door for him. Walking out of the alley, our pace slowed down at the same time. We looked at each other as if asking "Where to go?" But no one wanted to reveal this meaning, and we kept walking west without stopping.

"Let's go to the French Park." We began to look at the clouds in the sky, wondering if we were thinking that it wouldn't rain today.

"Do you have a pass?" The other person seemed to be moved.

I shook my head and fell silent again. Two bodies dragged forward non-stop, and we walked to the front of a green-walled cinema. People were crowding in in groups of three or five, and they didn't stop. We stared blankly at the huge pictures on the wall for a while, and involuntarily stepped on the stone steps, exchanging four dimes for two tickets in front of the ticket booth. When we went in, the movie had already started. Because we had been here several times, we naturally walked along the wall to the front. In the darkness, we were suddenly stopped by someone, "Four corners here." "Where are the two corners?" we asked.

"In the back."

"Changed the style?"

"Dancing today."

I looked at my friend, I guess he was looking at me too. In the darkness, no one could see anyone, and we retreated to the back and sat down. On the screen was a Western movie from five or six years ago; there were masked bandits, officers, girls, robberies, chases, making the audience in the whole courtyard laugh.

The movie ended inexplicably, followed by dancing. A large number of spectators flocked to the front at the same time, and several Boys stopped them. They could only stand at the very front of the two-corner seats.

Living beauties, fat jade legs, high breasts, tall and round hips, one by one moved onto the stage under the red lights. Fallen Russian nobles, they exposed their flesh, earning the laughter and applause of these spectators.

Squeezed out the door, it was a clear day, the sun shone on the ground and the shadows were scattered. I looked up, "It probably won't rain." That's what I thought in my heart.

Talks by a Japanese Returnee (2) 287

— Forget Me

In terms of accommodation, hotels in Tokyo cost at least four yuan per day, providing two meals. The quilts are mostly made of cotton, unlike the soft cotton quilts in our country, and their quilts are very thick. It's not very comfortable to use them occasionally, and it's easy to catch a cold. The floors are wiped very smoothly every day, and we may fall when we first go in. Bathhouses in Japan are very cheap, costing five cents each time, so they have developed a habit of liking to take baths. As for public items such as towels and soap, everyone has to bring their own to emphasize hygiene.

In terms of transportation, it is especially convenient in Tokyo. The so-called Dongyang cars (rickshaws) are taller than the ones here. The fare is about one yuan each time. The rickshaw pullers only need to pull two or three times a day and then they stop working. Cars are as dense as a net, soliciting business on the street. As long as you raise your hand to signal, the car will come over to pick you up, costing about fifty cents each time (equivalent to about half a yuan in China). Trams, no matter how far, cost only five cents. There are also elevated street railways, with train tracks erected above the air at every busy intersection. In addition, there are many underground railways, which, together with the large number of cars, will help in future wars. Moreover, the underground passages are very large. Once there is a war in Tokyo, they can also accommodate the city's elementary school students to continue their studies, which is not only convenient for transportation. Speaking of preparations for war, the Japanese are always looking at the bottom line. For example, the tall school buildings of elementary schools have flat roofs that are not intended to be used as playgrounds. In case of an emergency, anti-aircraft guns can be erected on top. Moreover, there must be an elementary school every so many roads. Recently, almost one elementary school is built every month. In this way, Tokyo's air defense facilities have become much more convenient.

Finally, let me say something about the virtues of the Japanese.

Japanese culture was originally passed down from China, so "respect" is highly valued. They not only respect people, but also respect gods. There are shrines everywhere, and everyone who passes by has to salute the shrine. And these so-called shrines are empty inside! Every loyal minister who has made contributions to the country, after his death, becomes another god, whom the people of the whole country admire. As for mud sculptures of Buddha statues, they certainly exist. The Japanese can also achieve the word "diligence," which can be seen from the recent progress. There are also many museums, zoos, botanical gardens, etc., which cultivate an interest in scientific research, so Japanese culture is a fusion of Chinese and Western cultures, and is the culture of a progressive country.

Amateur Mailbox

Living Together Until Old Age 288

Mr. Editor:

I have a matter concerning my friend, please reply in the Amateur Mailbox immediately after receiving this letter. Not only will my friend be grateful, but I will also be very grateful. Writing this, I respectfully wish you good health. Respectfully, Wen Hui.

My friend, Mr. Chen, is a former businessman who met an eighteen-year-old girl in February last year and fell in love with her; their feelings are very passionate. The girl's father passed away in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, and her mother, due to family circumstances, promised her daughter to a farmer in the same village as a child bride. At that time, she was married into the family as a child bride. Later, her husband's family decided on an auspicious day in October last year to get married. As soon as she got the news, she resisted vehemently and even wanted to commit suicide, but to no avail. She was forced by her mother and still married her fiancé involuntarily. Of course, the opinions of both parties are incompatible, so she is now determined to live together with my friend until old age, otherwise she would rather commit suicide. Please give me a complete solution to this difficult problem. The questions are:

(1) If my friend denies living together, how can it be resolved?

(2) Is it a crime for my friend to live together with her?

(3) What procedures should she go through to divorce her husband so that it can take effect?

(4) If she cannot leave my friend, what should she do?

Answer: This problem is very difficult to solve satisfactorily in the current society. Because first of all, it is very difficult for her to divorce her husband. There are two types of divorce: one is negotiated divorce, which means that she and her husband are both willing to divorce, which is relatively easy, but in fact her husband may not agree; the other is divorce by lawsuit, which requires the prior fulfillment of the legal conditions for divorce before it can proceed. According to what you said in your letter, she does not seem to have these conditions yet. As for living together or marrying your friend without getting a divorce, it is even more illegal. Therefore, if she is determined to live together with your friend until old age, but also wants to resolve it legally, I am afraid there is no hope.

So, what should they do? After thinking it over again and again, the editor believes that there are only two paths for them to take. First, although she hates her husband in her heart, if he does not abuse her too much and can get by, then she does not have to insist on living together with your friend. As long as the two of them can be spiritual friends and comfort each other, that is enough. Alternatively, if she really has reasons for not being able to continue living with her husband, then she should resolutely break away from her husband and unite with your friend. Of course, it is best to achieve the goal by proper means, but even if improper means are used, it cannot be said to be bad, and it should be used. Because this kind of marriage is originally unreasonable! Editor

Corrections to the False National Anthem 291

— Guang Han

Reading Li Huiying's "Half-Day Homework" in "Free Talk," I learned that the puppet Manchuria also produced a national anthem. The lyrics are like this:

Between heaven and earth, there is a new Manchuria:

New Manchuria, there is a new world,

Standing upright, without hardship or sorrow.

Only love creates a new country and

no grudges The people are 30 million,

Even if it is increased tenfold, you will still have freedom.

Value benevolence, and uphold courtesy so that I can cultivate myself.

The family is in order, the country is governed,

What else to ask for? Being near, we assimilate with the world,

Far away, we flow with heaven and earth.

It is said that this song was written by Zheng Xiaoxu. This old man's knowledge is well-founded, so what he writes is naturally vivid and colorful. Unfortunately, he has now lost his mind and is working hard as a slave to his master, so his wording is inevitably upside down and chaotic. Doesn't he know that the puppet country was created by the Japanese single-handedly, and the people of the Northeast are under double oppression, suffering great pain, so that they cannot sleep or eat in peace, and they cannot sit or lie down, and they sing about what "no hardship or sorrow" and what "also get freedom" are like deceptive words, which is extremely absurd! The two sentences, "The family is in order, the country is governed," are even more outrageous! Tens of millions of compatriots in the Northeast are personally tasting the bitterness of "family ruin and national death"! In order to make the name and reality match, I will now revise this false song. The words may not be as sophisticated as the old man Zheng, but the meaning is always more appropriate than his. The song says;

Between heaven and earth, there is a pseudo-Manchuria: In the pseudo-Manchuria, there is a false world;

The sky is dark and the earth is dark, and all kinds of misery and sorrow are known: The false country is created, the rights and interests overflow outwards, and the money flows eastward! The strong city has four provinces, and the people are 30 million,

It is difficult to get freedom with double oppression! The enemy's blood and the traitor's flesh must be eaten before we rest! The family is broken and the country is destroyed, where can this body stay! Today, we will endure humiliation with our compatriots, and tomorrow we will go to Japan to avenge our hatred!

Fiction

Between Flesh and Blood (3) 292

— Manzhi

Sixth Master didn't speak, only responded with a grunt, and lay down on the opium couch. The opium lamp was lit, and he picked up his pipe to smoke. Sixth Master was the most authoritative in the clan, so Lian Sun and Gui Sun didn't continue their earlier argument, but just sat in silence. The sound of rain outside the window and the sound of opium smoking inside the house resonated together. Second Master entered. He immediately saw Sixth Master smoking opium, walked closer to the opium couch, sat down, and lay down as well. Sixth Master caught sight of him from the corner of his eye, quickly took the pipe away, exhaled a puff of smoke, and called out, "Second Brother!" Then he took as thorough a puff as possible. After finishing the opium, Sixth Master sat up and said,

"Has Jian Guang returned?" Lian Sun asked in surprise.

Second Master didn't answer. In his heart, he remembered the incident from two years ago and still harbored resentment. Hearing Sixth Master's words, he thought that he still wanted to take in his rebellious son, and couldn't help but feel anger on top of his hatred. After a long while, he sat up from the opium couch. His beard was trembling, and his eyes were wide open. After another long while, he finally spoke.

"Sixth Master, can this kind of son still be taken in? Back when the peasant association was acting tyrannically, wasn't it him who shouted loudly at the farmers' rally in Dong Jiao Chang to overthrow the local tyrants and evil gentry, and to first overthrow Second Master Zhao Xian and Sixth Elder Yu Ting? Luckily, many of those beasts in human clothing have now been killed, and our Zheng family has what it has today! Now that he's back, if you don't put him to death, the Zheng family clan will not recognize you, Sixth Master, as Zheng!" As he spoke, he got off the opium couch and started pacing around the house.

The maidservant asked at the door to serve the meal, but Second Master was too angry to pay attention to her. The eldest young master, Lian Sun, hurried to the door and softly instructed to delay serving the meal, saying that there was something going on. A servant brought in a lamp, and the eldest young master, Lian Sun, took it and carried it into the house himself, placing it on the desk. The lamplight illuminated Second Master's body, and his shadow moved on the ground.

Sixth Master remained silent, hanging his head low. Second Master paced around the room and suddenly stopped, saying again,

"Report it to the county government quickly, and ask them to send a core team to your house to arrest him!" Only then did Sixth Master raise his head and say,

"I've also been thinking about that. However, this method is not very appropriate."

"Why is it not appropriate?" Second Master, thinking that Sixth Master was opposing his suggestion, questioned him with an arrogant tone.

"Second Brother knows that, because of this unfilial son of mine, the yamen back then threatened me, demanding three thousand taels of silver. Later, a lot of money was extorted. If he's said to have returned home this time, won't it cost more money again?"

"What money will it cost?"

"The core team that comes to the house to arrest him, it's unavoidable to give them some money for opium and alcohol. Moreover, I'm also afraid that those snake-eating, tiger-blood-drinking people will take the opportunity to take a few things from you!"

"Then... Sixth Master! What exactly do you intend to do?"
